or by negligence fail to prevent such animals from acting or performing in such a manner as to cause damage or unsanitary conditions to the property of another without the property owners permission public streets public parks and recreation areas or otherwise to cause a problem in the city acts deemed to be problems shall include but are not limited to the following 1 any dog or cat entering any place where food is stored prepared served or sold to the public except seeingeye dogs while in the company of a blind person 2 any dog while off its owners property or off of property which the owner has permission for the dog to be on chases runs after or jumps at pedestrians or vehicles moving on public streets sidewalks public ways and alleys 3 any dog or cat urinating or defecating or defacing or digging up property not owned by the dog or cats owner 4 any dog frequently howling yelping whining or barking in such manner as to unreasonably disturb any person or neighborhood 5 any dog or cat feeding from turning over or otherwise disturbing garbage containers not on its owners property 6 any dog snapping growling snarling jumping upon or otherwise threatening persons lawfully using public sidewalks streets alleys or public ways the snapping growling snarling provisions shall not apply to dogs that are securely fenced in on the owners property so that a reasonable person passing by would not perceive such conduct as an immediate threat to his safety or well being b a person who is offended by a problem animal shall call the aco and report such offending animal the aco shall upon receiving a complaint of a problem animal investigate the report and if same is well founded notify the animal owner of the complaint and request voluntary compliance of this article and report back to the person making the complaint if requested by the complaining party the aco shall not divulge the name of the complaining party to the animals owner c any owner who has custody of or owns an animal whose conduct would be classified as a problem under this section and who has previously been notified by the aco that his dog is a problem dog shall be dealt with in the same manner as provided for a violation of subsection 1484a any problem dog found running at large whose owner cannot be reasonably ascertained shall be taken directly to the pound  101893 a  odor from dogs it shall be unlawful and a nuisance for any person to keep on any tract lot or premises within the city any dog or group of dogs whether the same is housed in a fence pen kennel building or otherwise under such circumstances that the odor from such keeping interferes with the reasonable use and enjoyment of adjacent or neighboring premises  b  duty of owner for removal of feces it shall be the duty of the owner or personincharge of any dog to immediately remove and properly dispose of any feces deposited by said dog upon the grounds of any property within the city except for private property owned or controlled by the owner or personincharge of any such dog  c  confinement of female dogs in heat the owner shall keep leashed any female dog in heat or confine the dog within a building in such manner that the dog will not attract male dogs and will not be accessible to other dogs except for planned breeding  d  dogs causing damage it shall be unlawful for any person to own or harbor a dog that habitually trespasses on the property of persons other than the owner or person harboring the dog and causes damage thereto  e  owner liable for damages if the owner of a dog carelessly manages the dog or permits it to go at large and another person without fault on such other persons part suffers damage thereby such owner shall be liable for such damages  f  dog owners duty to remove overturned or scattered garbage it shall be the duty of the owner of any dog which has been allowed or suffered by such person to run at large to pick up and remove to a secure authorized container any garbage or refuse which such dog has caused to be overturned spilled or scattered upon any public or private property or upon any rightofway adjacent thereto upon demand from the owner or occupant thereof or upon demand of an animal control officer and it shall be unlawful for any such person to fail or refuse to do so  provided however that no prosecution shall be commenced and no arrest made pursuant to this section except upon affidavit made before and warrant issued by a duly appointed municipal judge or magistrate of the city  classification of dangerous animals a when any person claims that an animal is dangerous as defined under section 1482 he shall make a sworn statement before a sworn police officer of the city such statement shall specify the address or location of the alleged violation the nature time and date of the incident or acts the name and address of the owner if known and a description of the animal if known such statement shall be transmitted to the aco upon receipt of such statement the aco shall immediately make an investigation which such investigation must include an interview with the animals owner if the owner can be located the aco is also authorized to initiate investigation for violations under this section arising under other circumstances b upon a determination by the aco that an animal is dangerous the aco shall make a summary of findings which shall be incorporated in writing in a classification document the classification document shall order the owner to confine the animal in a substantial enclosure or to securely muzzle the animal and otherwise contain it in a reasonable manner as specified by the aco 1 the classification document shall be served upon the owner of the animal together with a copy of the procedure for appealing the classification service can be accomplished by hand delivery or by certified mail return receipt requested 2 the owner of any animal which is classified as dangerous may appeal the classification or any of its provisions to an appeals committee comprised of the police chief the aco and a licensed veterinarian designated by the mayor by notifying the chief in writing within 20 days of having been served such classification the aco shall within 20 days of receipt of such appeal notify the owner of the time and place of a hearing before the committee after conducting a hearing the committee shall take one of the following actions uphold modify or revoke the classification the decision shall be made in writing and a copy of the decision shall be mailed or personally delivered to the owner of the animal 3 any appeal of this decision must be made by written appeal within ten days of the date of such decision to the city council who shall hold a hearing at a designated time to decide whether to uphold modify or revoke the classification the owner shall have the right to appear in person with or without legal counsel and to put on any witnesses in defense to such classification  101893 dangerous animals a violation it shall be a violation of this article for any person to own keep maintain harbor or have custody of in the city any animal which the aco or upon appeal the hearing committees or the city council has classified dangerous as defined under this section unless such animal is securely muzzled or under restraint of a person by such means as specified in the classification document b notification all owners of animals classified dangerous shall immediately notify the aco when such animal is loose or unconfined  has bitten a human being or attacked another animal  was sold  given away  died or moved to another address 1 prior to a dangerous animal being sold or given away the present owner shall provide the name address and phone number of the new owner to the aco the new owner shall execute a document to be supplied by the aco acknowledging that such owner shall comply with the requirements of this article 2 as a condition to each animals classification each owner of a dangerous animal shall allow the aco to enter and inspect the owners premises to determine compliance with the classification document and this section c subsequent violation by an animal classified as dangerous 1 upon the written sworn affidavit of any person or upon a written finding of the aco setting forth that an animal previously classified as dangerous has actually bitten another animal or a person while in violation of the provisions of the classification document the aco may impound and subsequently destroy such animal whether such animal shall then be at large or in its owners custody 2 prior to the actual impoundment of any dog securely confined to an owners property and prior to any destruction of any animal classified as dangerous under this article the aco shall seek from the circuit court of barbour county alabama a court order permitting the destruction of the animal the complaint shall be an in rem proceeding with notice given to the dogs owner at least seven days prior to the date set for the hearing the owner can appear at the hearing to produce evidence to show why such dog should not be destroyed appeal from the court order shall be as other appeals from the circuit court the requirement to obtain a court order can be waived in writing by the owner thus allowing the immediate destruction of the dog  101893 cruelty to animals a whoever 1 impounds or confines any animal in any place and fails to supply the animal during such confinement with a sufficient quantity of good and wholesome food and water  2 keeps any animal in any enclosure without wholesome exercise and change of air  3 abandons to die any animal that is maimed sick infirmed or diseased shall be in violation of this section b a person who unnecessarily overloads overdrives tortures torments deprives of necessary sustenance or shelter or unnecessarily or cruelly beats mutilates or kills any animal or causes the same to be done or carries in or upon any vehicle or otherwise any animal in a cruel or inhumane manner shall be in violation of this section c whoever exposes deposits or puts out upon his or her own premises or upon the premises of another or upon property owned by the city or any other governmental unit or agency or upon any street alley lane highway and thoroughfare of any kind any substance known to be poisonous to animals which is poured over wrapped in or otherwise combined with food with the intent of enticing such animals to eat such poisonous substance and become poisoned thereby shall be in violation of this section intent to poison shall be presumed as a matter of law where poison is found mixed with any type of food the finding of such poisonous substance or poisoned food together with the proof as to the identity of the person exposing depositing or putting out same shall be prima facie evidence of the intent to poison and destroy such animals this section shall not apply where insect or rodent poison is used on a persons own premise for control of insects mice or rodents in accordance with the manufacturers instructions  101893 abandonment of animals a any person who is the owner or possessor or has charge or custody of any animal or who abandons any animal in a street road or public place without providing for the care sustenance protection and shelter of such animal shall be in violation of this section b upon an affidavit of any person or a law enforcement officer stating an animal appears to have been abandoned the aco will investigate the matter and thereupon is authorized to impound and dispose of the animal in the manner provided by this article with the assistance of a law enforcement officer if necessary the aco shall cause written notice bearing the address where the animal may be claimed by the owner thereof and the time by which the animal must be claimed to be sent to the owner if known at the last known address  101893 animals in vehicles a no vehicle owner passenger or operator shall place or confine an animal or allow it to be placed or confined or to remain in an unattended motor vehicle without sufficient ventilation or under conditions or for such a period of time as may reasonably be expected to endanger the health or wellbeing of such animal due to heat lack of water or such other circumstances as may be expected to cause suffering disability or death b no operator of a motor vehicle shall allow an animal to be unattended while in the vehicle unless the animal is securely restrained so that a reasonable person passing by would not perceive such animal as an immediate threat to his safety or wellbeing  101893 impoundment a animals of the following classes may be captured and impounded immediately wherever located within the areas of the city subject to this article 1 subject to the restrictions contained in subsection 1487c2 dangerous animals of all kinds  2 any dog or cat whose owner cannot produce evidence of the rabies vaccination tag upon request of the aco  3 abandoned animals and animals whose ownership is unknown and are commonly referred to as strays whether running by itself or in a pack  4 any animal running at large in violation of section 1484  5 female dogs and cats in breeding season not confined to the premises of the owners in such manner as to avoid nuisances and to prevent access to other animals  6 any animal that is infected or reasonably believed to be infected with a contagious or infectious disease to humans or animals b the aco and its animal control officers law enforcement officers and humane officers or state charted nonprofit humane organizations shall subject to the procedural requirements in this article have authority to pick up catch or procure and impound any animal in violation of this chapter or any animal infected or believed to be infected with rabies or other contagious or infectious disease to humans or animals in such a manner as is reasonably necessary to effectuate its capture impounded animals shall be confined in a human manner at an animal shelter c an impounded animal with a name plate current license or rabies tag shall be held for at least five days  without a name plate current license or rabies tag or collar an impounded animal shall be held for three business days including the day of impoundment except that a sick or injured animal which poses a threat to the safety of the personnel responsible for the care of such animal may be euthanized at the discretion of the impounding agency a reasonable effort shall be made by the aco to locate the owner of any impounded dog or cat however if any impounded dog has a rabies tag on its collar and the owner cannot be contacted the aco shall contact the dogs veterinarian and with the veterinarians permission deliver the animal to him for boarding with the owner being responsible to the veterinarian for the boarding bill the depositing of a letter of notification by first class us mail shall constitute adequate notification of impoundment the owner shall also be notified by phone if reasonably feasible this section shall not apply to animals surrendered by the owner or an agent of the owner in which case disposition may be made as provided in this article without notification or a holding period and without obtaining a court order at the expiration of the holding period the animal may be disposed of in a manner provided in this chapter d a registry shall be maintained by the impounding agency the registry shall contain identifying characteristics of each animal impounded along with the location date and reason of each pickup  101893     82195 redemption and disposition of animals all animals which have been impounded in accordance with the provisions of this article may be disposed of as provided below every attempt shall be made by the animal control division to treat animals in the citys care in a humane manner and to strive toward the adoption of animals whenever possible 1 within the holding period animals except dangerous and vicious animals may be redeemed by the owner or his agent upon the payment of those fees or costs associated with the impoundment as established by the city council the owner entitled to possession of an impounded dog or cat which does not have the required rabies inoculation certificate and tag shall be able to take possession of the animal after presenting proper identification the city will provide the rabies inoculation whenever possible and the owner will remit the cost of such to the city along with payment of other associated costs for impoundment of the animal 2 if not redeemed within the holding period animals may be disposed of by humane euthanasia 3 those animals which would otherwise be disposed of by euthanasia may be offered to state chartered nonprofit humane organizations for the purpose of providing adoption of such animals fees and costs shall be waived for the disposition of animals in this manner all dogs and cats placed with this organization shall be vaccinated before the organization offers each animal for adoption 4 animals remaining in the pound for ten days which have not been redeemed by their owners shall be available for private sale or adoption by the animal control officer by after having first given notice of the date such animal is available for sale or adoption a full description of the animal for sale shall be posted for at least seven days no animal shall be sold for less than $1500 any dog or cat not sold sale or adoption may be sold to the auburn university of veterinary medicine for $1500  101893 fees and charges  administration any cat or dog except a dangerous dog impounded hereunder may be reclaimed as herein provided upon payment by the owner of the following fees 1 boarding fee charged by the city at the rate of $400 for each day of impoundment plus a tendollar impoundment fee or the actual costs of boarding charged by an other state chartered nonprofit organization or veterinarian or kennel designated by the city council 2 the amount of vaccination fee if necessary  101893   82195 enforcement a the mayor shall police department appoint an aco to take charge of the animal control division the aco shall along with his assistants enforce the provisions of this article the aco shall have the authority to issue a citation to aid in the enforcement of the provisions of this article b subject to the limitations and restrictions contained in this article the aco his assistants and members of the police division shall have the right for the protection of public health welfare and safety to enter upon any property within the city for the purpose of capturing and impounding any animal which is in violation of this chapter c any expense incurred in the handling of any animal under the provisions of this chapter shall be borne by the owner or custodian of such animal if same can be ascertained d it shall be a violation of this section to interfere with any animal control officer while in the lawful performance of his duties or with anyone who may be assisting in the performance of such duties e any person who willfully refuses to sign and accept a citation issued by a law enforcement officer shall be in violation of this chapter f the city council may contract with any state chartered nonprofit humane organization or veterinarian to carry out all or part of the duties herein such organization or individual shall carry out the duties pursuant to the provisions prescribed in this article failure to do so shall result in the city council assuming the duties or contracting with another organization or individual to assume the duties compensation may be provided in an adequate amount to fulfill the prescribed duties  101893  iii 7201 enforcement of penalties for violation a enforcement of this chapter shall be by summons and complaint as provided for in section 113 b any person convicted of violating any provision of this chapter within a 12month period shall be guilty of a violation and shall be guilty of a violation and shall be punished as follows 1 for a first violation a fine of $2000 2 for a second violation a fine of $5000 3 for a third violation a fine of $10000 4 for a fourth or any subsequent violation a fine in an amount not exceeding $50000 or imprisonment of not more than six months or both such fine and imprisonment at the discretion of the municipal judge trying the case any person who has been charged with the violation of any provision of this article except those offenses identified in section 1487 1488 and 1489 and who desires to waive trial of the question of his guilt or innocence of such alleged offense may pay the fine prescribed above to the municipal court of the city and the municipal court magistrate is hereby authorized and instructed to receive such amount voluntary settlement shall not be permitted to any person who has been twice convicted of the same offense prior to the date of the instant alleged offense and such person shall be required to stand trial in municipal court offenses not settled as provided in this subsection prior to the court appearance date shown on the notice of violation will be disposed of in the same manner as is any other case appearing on the regular municipal court docket this provision shall be considered as part of the city of eufaulas extended schedule of fines pursuant to rule 20c arja c any person who is alleged to have committed any of the following offenses listed in this chapter shall be required to stand trial in municipal court harboring dangerous animals cruelty to animals abandonment of animals any person convicted of any act listed in this subsection b shall be punished by a fine of not more than $50000 or imprisonment of not more than six months or both such fine and imprisonment at the discretion of the municipal judge trying the case d in addition to the penalties provided in this section the city council is hereby authorized to institute any appropriate action or proceeding including suit for injunctive relief in order to abate violations of this chapter  101893  iii 7201   confinement of animals known or suspected to have rabies it shall be unlawful for any person to keep harbor or maintain on or about any place or premises in the city a dog or other animal which is known to have or reasonably suspected of having rabies unless such animal is securely confined in such a manner as to effectively prevent contact with or injury to persons or other animals any such animal not so confined shall either be destroyed or removed to the city pound or other appropriate place by the chief of police or other person designated for that purpose by the city and there securely confined  confinement of animals bitten by suspected animals it shall be unlawful for any person to keep harbor or maintain on or about any place or premises in the city a dog cat or any other animal whatsoever which has been or is reasonably suspected to have been bitten or otherwise injured by or in contact with another animal afflicted with or suspected of being afflicted with rabies in such a manner as to permit or favor transmission of such disease unless such dog cat or other animal so bitten injured or in contact shall be securely confined for not less than six months thereafter  authority to confine suspect animals  interference  duty to destroy afflicted animals a the animal control officer shall have the right at any time to move or cause to be moved to the city pound or other place designated by him for observation or examination any dog cat or other animal which is reasonably suspected to be afflicted with rabies or which has bitten or otherwise injured a human being in such a manner as would permit or favor the transmission of the virus of rabies if such animal should be afflicted with rabies or which has been or is reasonably suspected to have been bitten or injured or in contact with another animal afflicted or reasonably suspected of being afflicted with rabies b it shall be unlawful for any person to hinder obstruct or interfere with the animal control officer or any authorized agent or deputy in the exercise of the authority conferred upon him in this section c it shall be the duty of the animal secs 18571875  reserved article iv  electrical code division 1  generally purpose  scope a the purpose of this article is the practical safeguarding of persons and of buildings and their contents from hazards arising from the use of electricity b the provisions of this article shall apply to every electrical installation including alterations repairs and equipment within or connected to the electrical system of the city except as may be specifically exempted in this article  penalties any person who violates the provisions of this article shall be subject to punishment as prescribed in section 16 c secs 18781890  reserved division 2  administration and enforcement subdivision i  general provisions obedience to inspectors orders it shall be unlawful for any person to fail or refuse to obey any order of the electrical inspector issued under the provisions of this article and such person shall be subject to the penalty prescribed in section 16  denial of entry for inspector it shall be unlawful for any person to refuse entry to the electrical inspector when he is performing the duties prescribed in this article and such person shall be subject to the penalty prescribed in section 16  conflict of interest of inspectors no officer or employee connected with the electrical inspectors office shall be financially interested in the furnishing of labor materials or appliances for the construction alteration or maintenance of electrical installations or in the making of plans or specifications therefor unless such person is the owner of such building no employee shall engage in any work which is inconsistent with his duties or with the interest of the inspectors office  disputes  appeals any dispute between the electrical inspector while in the performance of his duties and any person shall be presented to the electrical board for settlement if no settlement is made either party may request a board of arbitration to be formed in which case each party to the dispute shall select one arbitrator and these two shall select a third member the decision of the board of arbitration shall be final and binding upon all parties unless appealed to the city council decisions of the city council may be appealed to courts having jurisdiction any action shall stand unless and until reversed by a higher authority  830 discontinuance of electrical service for noncompliance for failure to comply with this article the electrical inspector shall after due notice order discontinuance of electrical service to the locality of the building concerned and shall enforce such discontinuance until there is compliance with the requirements of this article a secs 189618105  reserved subdivision ii  electrical board footnotes  2  cross reference boards commissions and authorities  2241 et seq created  membership a there is created for the city an electrical board to be composed of five members b the board shall be composed of a representative of the power supply company two master electricians one electrical engineer registered professional and the electrical inspector for the city such members to be appointed by the mayor and council the members shall be citizens of the city at least 25 years of age and in addition electricians shall have had at least five years experience as master electricians c the members shall serve staggered terms of four years each except for position number 1 the positions qualifications and terms of office shall be as follows 1 position number 1 city electrical inspector term to expire november 1 of each year 2 position number 2 master electrician term to expire  and november 1 of each fourth year thereafter 3 position number 3 representative of the power supply company term to expire  and november 1 of each fourth year thereafter 4 position number 4 master electrician term to expire  and november 1 of each fourth year thereafter 5 position number 5 electrical engineer term to expire  and november 1 of each fourth year thereafter d the members may at any time be removed by the city council initial terms of office shall begin immediately upon the city councils appointment of initial members whenever a vacancy shall occur the city council shall appoint a new member to the board to fill the unexpired term 21 secretary the electrical inspector shall serve as secretary of the electrical board he shall advise the board in all matters under discussion and he shall have the same voting power as any other member of the board 22 organization the electrical board shall establish all rules and procedures necessary to conduct the business of the board the board shall elect one member to serve as chairman and all proceedings shall be subject to approval by the city council 23 compensation the members of the electrical board shall serve without compensation 24 meetings the electrical board shall meet at least twice yearly and shall meet at any time on 24 hours notice by the chairman 25 filling vacancies any vacancy on the electrical board shall be filled in the manner prescribed for the member so vacating 26 quorum three members of the electrical board shall constitute a quorum for the conduct of business 27 powers and duties a administration the electrical board shall be considered as the administrative authority supervising the enforcement of this article b certification 1 application for certificate the board shall prescribe the manner and form of application for a certificate to engage in the installation and maintenance of electrical wiring and equipment 2 examination an examination for electrical certification shall be held on the date set by the board and not less than once every three months if requested 3 issuance of certificate the board shall if satisfied with the results of such examination issue a certificate of a style and form determined by the board in the name of the person so examined c hearings on charges of violations the board shall have the power and duty to receive and consider all charges of violation of this article and to conduct hearings on all such matters charges shall be in writing and a copy of the charges shall be attached to a notice to appear before the board and be served to the person so charged at least 48 hours before such hearing both the city and the person charged shall have the right to introduce evidence and to appear by counsel if the person filing the charges or the person so charged is also a member of the board the member shall have no vote in the proceedings d interpretations of technical matters in disputes charges arising from disputes over interpretation of technical sections of this article shall be dealt with in the manner described in sections 1894 and 18197 e suspension of certificates the board may either suspend or revoke the certificate of the person charged if it after such a hearing deems him guilty of the charges preferred f recommendation of amendments the board shall consider and recommend all matters relating to any amendment of this article to the city and the members of the city council g grants of special permission the board shall meet and pass or deny on all matters related to special permission contemplated by the electrical code 28 secs 1811418125  reserved subdivision iii  permits inspections and certificate permit required nonresidential installation originating from an overhead electrical system must be in rigid metallic conduit up to the distribution panel service entrance conductors from an underground electric supply system may be either rigid metallic conduit or pvc conduit up to the distribution panel all other conductors must be in metallic or pvc conduit except that service entrance cable may be installed as a service conductor in apartment houses residences and farm buildings additional appropriate size copper grounding conductor must be used when pvc or metallic conduit is being utilized all conduit runs shall contain a green grounding conductor of appropriate size complete and continuous grounding must be maintained for the total installation 2 switchboard and panel boards a each used as a residence when the service has to be changed c when rewiring a building that is being renovated all wiring for new construction additions shall conform to this article 5 low voltage circuits standards for master electrician a master electrician shall be a person who is competent to engage in all electrical matters within the scope of this article and to supervise others in such matters  duties and responsibilities of master electricians a supervision master electricians shall install or supervise the installation of all electrical wiring and equipment and alterations to wiring and equipment within the scope of this article b compliance master electricians employed by an electrical contractor duly qualified under this article shall have final responsibility for compliance with or violations of all provisions of this article for all work done or equipment installed c reporting the ordering of work in violation if an owner employer or any person of authority over a master electrician shall order work done or equipment installed that violates the provisions of this article it shall be the duty of the master electrician to immediately notify in writing the electrical inspector of all particulars concerning the violation d application for permit it shall be the duty of the master electrician to apply for all permits to install or alter electrical wiring or equipment within the scope of this article and before applying for such permit the master electrician shall determine that the work or equipment contemplated is in compliance with the provisions of this article and shall furnish with his application all information requested by the electrical inspector e request for inspection the master electrician shall determine when work as required by the electrical inspector is ready for inspection and shall notify the electrical inspectors office for the inspection the master electrician shall further notify the electrical inspectors office at the completion of any electrical installation within the scope of this article f compliance with notice from inspector upon notice from the electrical inspector that any part of the wiring or equipment inspected is not acceptable under the provisions of this article the master electrician in charge or the owner or the owners agent shall upon completion of such changes so notify the inspector abatement division 1  reserved footnotes  7  editors note  2 adopted  repealed ch 18 div 1  18326 in its entirety formerly said section pertained to unsafe building abatement code  adopted and derived from  6192 secs 1832618340  reserved division 2  demolition of unsafe structures generally the city shall have authority after notice provided for in this division to move or demolish buildings and structures or parts of buildings and structures party walls and foundations when the same are found by the governing body of the city to be unsafe to the extent of being a public nuisance from any cause art iii1 102097 meaning of appropriate city official  duties  notice of unsafe or dangerous condition the term appropriate city official as used in this article shall mean any city building official or deputy and any other city official or city employee designated by the mayor or other chief executive officer of the city as the person to exercise the authority and perform the duties delegated by this article to appropriate city official whenever the appropriate city official of the city shall find that any building structure part of building or structure party wall or foundation situated in any city is unsafe to the extent that it is a public nuisance the official shall report the findings to the city governing body at that time the city governing body shall determine whether the building structure part of building or structure party wall or foundation constitutes a public nuisance should the city governing body find by resolution that the building structure part of building or structure party wall or foundation is a public nuisance then the appropriate city official shall give the person or persons firm association or corporation last assessing the property for state taxes by certified or registered mail to the address on file in the revenue commissioners office notice to remedy the unsafe or dangerous condition of the building or structure or to demolish the same within a reasonable time set out in the notice which time shall not be less than 30 days unless an extension is granted by the appropriate city official or suffer the building or structure to be demolished by the city and the cost thereof assessed against the property the mailing of the certified or registered notice properly addressed and postage prepaid shall constitute notice as required in this division the city shall place a sign or placard within 15 feet of the entrance of the building or structure indicating that the city had declared the building or structure to be a public nuisance  however if there is no entrance in which to place the sign or placard then the sign or placard may be posted at any location upon the building or structure art iii2 102097 hearing procedure  order  appeal a within the time specified in the notice but not more than 30 days from the date the notice is given any person firm or corporation having an interest in the building or structure may file a written request for a hearing before the governing body of the city together with the objections to the finding by the city governing body that the building or structure is unsafe to the extent of becoming a public nuisance the filing of the request shall hold in abeyance any action on the finding of the city governing body until a determination thereon is made by the city governing body the hearing shall be held not less than five nor more than 30 days after the request in the event that no hearing is timely requested the governing body shall order the building or structure to be demolished the demolition may be accomplished at the option of the city by the use of its own forces or it may provide by contract for the demolition for purposes of this article compliance with the competitive bid laws are not required the city shall have authority to sell or otherwise dispose of salvaged materials resulting from the demolition b any person aggrieved by the decision of the governing body at the hearing may within ten days thereafter appeal to the circuit court upon filing with the clerk of the court notice of appeal and bond for security of costs in the form and amount to be approved by the circuit clerk upon filing of the notice of appeal and approval of the bond the clerk of the court shall serve a copy of the notice of appeal on the clerk of the city and the appeal shall be docketed in the court and shall be a preferred case therein the clerk of the city shall upon receiving the notice file with the clerk of the court a copy of the findings and determination of the governing body in proceedings and trials shall be held without jury upon the determination of the governing body that the building or structure is unsafe to the extent that it is a public nuisance art iii3 102097 report of cost of demolition  adoption of resolution fixing costs  proceeds of sale of salvaged materials  objections to findings of cost  notice upon demolition of the building or structure the appropriate city official shall make an itemized written report to the governing body of the cost thereof the cost of the demolition shall be the actual cost the city incurs in the demolition should the city use its own forces including administrative costs the city incurs in abating the nuisance should the city contract for demolition the cost shall be the actual cost the contractor charges the city for the demolition including administrative costs the city incurs in abating the nuisance upon the report of the costs by the appropriate city official the governing body shall adopt a resolution fixing the costs which it finds were incurred in the demolition and assessing the same against the property  provided however the proceeds of any moneys received from the use of salvaged materials from the building or structure shall be used or applied against the cost of the demolition  and provided further then any person firm or corporation having an interest in the property may be heard at the meeting concerning the fixing of the costs or the amounts thereof the city clerk shall give at least ten days notice of the meeting at which the fixing of the costs is to be considered by firstclass mail to all entities having an interest in the property whose address and interest is determined from the revenue commissioners records on the property or is otherwise known to the clerk the fixing of costs by the governing body shall constitute a special assessment against the lot or lots parcel or parcels of land upon which the building or structure was located and thus made and confirmed shall constitute lien on the property for the amount of the assessment the lien shall be superior to all other liens on the property except liens for taxes and shall continue in force until paid a certified copy of the resolution shall be filed in the office of the judge of probate of barbour county upon filing the revenue commissioner of the county shall add the amount of the lien to the ad valorem tax bill on the property and shall collect the amount as if it were a tax and remit the amount to the city the county revenue commissioner shall retain ten percent of the amount of each lien collected to be used for operational purposes art iii4 102097 assessment of costs  sale and redemption of lots the city shall have the power to assess the costs authorized for in this division against any lot or lots parcel or parcels of land purchased by the state at any sale for nonpayment of taxes and where any assessment is made against the lot or lots parcel or parcels of the land a subsequent redemption thereof by any person authorized to redeem or sale thereof by the state shall not operate to discharge or in any manner affect the lien of the city for the assessment but any redemptioner or purchaser at any sale by the state of any lot or lots parcel or parcels of land upon which an assessment has been levied whether prior to or subsequent to sale to the state for the nonpayment of taxes shall take the same subject to the assessment the assessment shall then be added to the tax bill of the property collected as a tax and remitted to the city art iii5 102097 payment of assessments payment of any assessment or if delinquent the collection of the assessment shall be made in the manner and as provided for the payment of municipal improvement assessments as provided for the payment of and delinquent collection of municipal improvement assessments pursuant to ala 197  11481 et seq the city may in the latter notice elect to have the revenue commissioner collect the assessment by adding the same to the tax bill  upon the election the revenue commissioner shall collect the assessment using all methods available for collecting ad valorem taxes ten percent of the amount of each assessment collected by the county revenue commissioner shall be retained by the county revenue commissioner and used for operational drainage waters minimum diameter of pipe shall be 18 inches and be class three concrete pipe metal pipe or hdpe may be substituted for concrete pipe if hdpe pipe is used the ends shall be protected by operate a business involving the use of one or more horsedrawn carriages on the streets of the city unless a business license for such business has first been granted by the city in accordance with the provisions of city ordinances the business license shall be $5000 per carriage and be effective only for the calendar year stated in the document unless suspended or revoked sooner as provided by ordinance 2 application for the business license shall be made on forms provided by the city clerk and shall provide such information as is required for other business license applications and such additional information as may be necessary to define completely the business operation renewal of the business license shall be required prior to january 31 of each year b fixed place of business required  each horsedrawn carriage company as a condition for holding a license under the provisions of this article and the business license ordinance shall establish and maintain a fixed headquarters on private property for the operation of the companys business  the headquarters to conform to the ordinances of the city and shall provide adequate offstreet parking space for all horsedrawn carriages not in service on the streets the company headquarters shall not be moved except by the approved transfer of the companys license to another location  records a each animaldrawn carriage operator shall maintain at a single location business records of its animaldrawn carriage business the records must contain the following information at a minimum 1 an identification of the carriage used for each trip  2 the number of trips made by each carriage on a daily basis  3 the number of passengers per trip on a daily basis  and 4 an identification of the animal used for each trip and a statement of the periods of work and rest for each b records shall be made available for inspection when requested by the city  insurance a indemnity for benefit of city  any horsedrawn carriage company operating under this article shall hold the city its officers agents servants and employees harmless against any and all liability loss damages or expense which may accrue to the city by reason of negligence default or misconduct of the company in connection with the rights granted to such company hereunder the city shall be named as an additional insured on all public liability insurance instruments nothing in this article shall be considered to make the city its officers agents servants or employees liable for damages because of any negligent act or omission or commission by any horsedrawn carriage business or operation by the company of a horsedrawn carriage business or service either in respect to injury to persons or with respect to damage to property which may be sustained b insurance for benefit of passengers andor the general public  any horsedrawn carriage company desiring a business license to do business shall give and maintain a policy of indemnity from an insurance company authorized to do business in the state for each vehicle in use as a horsedrawn carriage the minimum coverage shall be $10000000 for bodily injury to any one person $30000000 for injury to more than one person which are sustained in the same accident and $2500000 for property damage resulting from one accident the indemnity insurance shall insure to the benefit of any person who shall be injured or who shall sustain damage to property caused by the negligence of a horsedrawn carriage company its servants or agents c blanket policy  any company or person operating a horsedrawn carriage in the city shall obtain a separate horsedrawn carriage policy of indemnity insurance except where such company or person actually owns or holds legal title to more than horsedrawn carriage in which event such company or person may give one policy of indemnity insurance covering all the horsedrawn carriages who may be jointly operating or doing business under a licensed horsedrawn carriage name d notice when policy of insurance is changed or voided  before any policy of insurance required by this article is voided for any cause nonpayment of premium or otherwise notice thereof shall be given in writing to the city clerk at least five days before the same shall take effect any change in the policy or insurer requires immediate notification in writing to the city clerk  chauffers license a license required  no person shall operate a horsedrawn carriage for hire upon the streets of the city and no person who owns or operates a horsedrawn carriage company shall permit a horsedrawn carriage to be driven and no horsedrawn carriage operating under a horsedrawn carriage company approved by the city shall be driven at any time for hire unless the driver of the horsedrawn carriage shall first have obtained and shall have then in force a chauffers license issued under this article and a current motor vehicle operators license issued by the state except out of state students and military and that the license is not under suspension or revocation to that end applicant must provide a recent motor vehicle operator record of convictions at the time of application b examination of applicant  issuance or denial of license  it shall be the duty of the risk manager or hisher designee to examine the applicant hisher reference police and traffic record and the other vouchers and thereafter to either grant or refuse the license c license to be displayed in horsedrawn carriage  the chauffers license issued under the provisions of this article shall be placed on display in the horsedrawn carriage to be operated by the holder of the license where the license will be in clear view of the passengers at all times when the horsedrawn carriage is for hire d alteration of license prohibited  it shall be prohibited for any person to willfully alter deface obliterate or destroy a chauffers license or cause or allow the same e license not transferable  any chauffers license issued under this article is not transferable and is to be used solely by the person to whom it is issued and the company for which it is issued d duration of license  the chauffers license is $2500 and is renewable on an annual basis effective on january 31 of each year license may be renewed upon presentation of a current motor vehicle record physicians statement and criminal background investigation report or sworn statement unless the license for the preceding period has been revoked or is under suspension  drug testing each horsedrawn carriage company or operator shall establish and maintain a drug testing program for all employees in safetysensitive positions to include all drivers the program shall include preemployment random postaccident and probable cause testing records of testing shall be maintained by the employer and shall be made available for inspection by the risk manager or hisher designee or any state or federal regulatory enforcement officials  vehicle requirements a identification and marking generally  every horsedrawn carriage shall have a permanent sign on the vehicle either painted or adhesivebacked decals containing the full name of the horsedrawn carriage company operating the vehicle b safe mechanical condition of horsedrawn carriage required  every horsedrawn carriage operated on the streets of the city shall be maintained in a safe mechanical condition with all safety related equipment remaining intact and operable at all times when the horsedrawn carriage is in service c carriage lubrication  wheels  carriages must be kept properly lubricated and wheels must spin freely and straight d cleanliness of horsedrawn carriage required  each vehicle operating under this article shall be kept painted and in a clean and sanitary condition free of litter and debris and at all times suitable for public transportation of passengers e vehicle inspection required  each horsedrawn carriage shall be inspected by the risk manager or hisher designee for the compliance with the provision of the article and shall pass the inspection before the vehicle may be used as a horsedrawn carriage in the city periodic inspections will be required twice a year at a time and place as directed by the risk manager or hisher designee each horsedrawn carriage shall be subject to random inspections without notice to insure continued compliance with the provisions of this article f rates of fare  rate posting required  no owner or driver of a horsedrawn carriage shall charge a greater sum for the use of the horsedrawn carriage than in accordance with rates authorized by the city rates shall be displayed so as to be conspicuous at the stand andor on the vehicle g safety equipment required  each horsedrawn carriage shall be equipped with electrically powered lights or lanterns and reflectors which shall be in use when operating during the hours of darkness and when raining the lights and reflectors shall be mounted so that they are visible from a distance of 500 feet in any direction reflective devices are to be worn by the horse h brakes  carriages are to be equipped with a working mechanical brake that will prevent movement when slowing stopping and parked i slowmoving vehicle emblem  each carriage shall be equipped with a rearfacing slowmoving vehicle emblem that can be seen from a minimum distance of 500 feet  requirements for animals in service operating regulations  in addition to the business license imposed herein and by the business license ordinance no license shall be permitted any carriage operator unless the operator complies with division ii of the animal ordinance ch 14 and the following regulations 1 a licensed veterinarian shall certify after due and proper inspection the good health of each draft animal before it is placed into service a minimum of two such health inspections shall be required for each animal each calendar year  to be performed during the months of january and july with copies submitted to the city risk management department 2 no single animal shall pull a carriage holding more than ten people including the driver two horses cannot pull more than the seating capacity of the carriage 3 animals shall wear properly attached and fitted blinders while pulling carriages 4 carriages shall not be pulled by stallions or pregnant mares 5 unless written approval is given by a licensed veterinarian no animal having open sores or wounds or any disease or ailment shall be permitted to be in service on the streets of the city 6 each draft animal shall have its hooves properly trimmed and shod for street surfaces being maintained by a farrier at least every eight weeks or as necessary a record of farrier service shall be maintained for inspection 7 temporary shoes can only be used if the horse has thrown a shoe during a tour and then only to get the horse back to the barn to be shoed 8 each animal shall be groomed daily and not have fungus dandruff or a dirty coat 9 flies and other insects must be controlled sanitation and other necessary means 10 harnesses shall be properly fitted maintained and oiled so that no irritating material will come in direct contact with the animal 11 no driver may use more than a light touch of the whip upon any animal and no driver or other person may forcefully strike an animal or make movements or noise intended to frighten or harm an animal no animal shall be made to perform by means of any prod stick electrical shock physical force or by causing pain or discomfort 12 no driver shall permit an animal to pull a carriage at a speed faster than a slow trot except in emergency situations 13 no animal shall be subject to any condition or treatment whether in service or out of service which will impair the good health and physical condition of that animal 14 no animal shall be worked more than eight hours in any 24hour period without ten minutes of rest for each 50 minutes of work and with a minimum of 12 consecutive hours of rest 15 animals shall not be overridden or driven to overheating or exhaustion 16 the risk manager or hisher designee shall be empowered to inspect all stables and operating facilities of any carriage company without notices and to examine operating practices of any carriage company to ensure continuous compliance with this article 17 any applicant who refuses or fails to comply with the requirements of this article shall not be issued a business license until proof of compliance is presented by the applicant and certified by the risk manager the foregoing licensing requirements shall be ongoing as requirements for continuous operation 18 the mayor may upon recommendation of the risk manager or hisher designee temporarily suspend a license or carriage company operation for violation of the provisions of this article and may be subject to revocation action as provided by the business license ordinance  stands generally a no parking shall be permitted in the corporate limits of the city except at such stands as may be established by the city horsedrawn carriage stands shall be designated by signs fees for the use of the stands may be established by the mayor or hisher designee b drivers of horsedrawn carriages operated under this article shall maintain stands in a sanitary condition at all times  driver requirements generally a driver not to leave vehicle while waiting to be hired  it is prohibited for any driver of any horsedrawn carriage to leave the vehicle or the immediate premises thereof while the vehicle is parked while waiting to be hired b use of alcohol or drugs  any driver of any horsedrawn carriage is prohibited from consuming or being under the influence of alcohol or illegal drugs while operating a carriage while waiting to operate a carriage or while onduty generally use of prescription and overthecounter drugs which affect the drivers ability to operate a horsedrawn carriage is prohibited during onduty hours c operation with animals under control  due to the nature of operating animaldrawn vehicles in areas of congestion and heavy traffic within the city it shall be prohibited to operate the animaldrawn vehicles except when the animals are under complete control at all times and shall be operated with extra caution and due care for the safety of others d obeying traffic laws  the operation of the animaldrawn vehicles shall be in accordance with all state and local traffic laws and ordinances animaldrawn carriages shall be prohibited from stopping on any street for the purpose of loading or unloading passengers during the course of a tour except when stopping to allow other vehicles to pass or pedestrians to cross unless directed to stop by a police officer  hours of operation a no horsedrawn carriage shall be operated on the city streets between the hours of  midnight and  am on any day no carriage shall be operated for hire between the hours of  pm and  pm monday except that such restriction shall not apply on legal holidays b when weather conditions are adverse or inclement which could harm either animals or passengers carriages shall not be operated c while in motion carriage lights must be lit from onehalf hour before dusk until such time as night operations cease carriage lights shall be lit during inclement weather  sanitation requirements a manure and urine must be immediately treated with a chemical deodorizing solution and manure must be removed immediately from the street by the carriage company b horse diapers or other sanitary devices which prevent excrement from being deposited on the street surface must be approved for efficiency by the risk manager or hisher designee  impediment of traffic flow it shall be prohibited for any animaldrawn carriage to willfully impede the normal flow of traffic on any city street alley or thoroughfare at any time animaldrawn carriages will be required to pull immediately to the nearest curb area when one or more vehicles are unable to safely pass or continue in normal traffic flow  accidents a the driver of an animaldriven carriage shall report any accident involving such carriage to the police department at the time of the accident b no animal or carriage involved in an accident where structural damage to the carriage or injury to the animal has occurred shall be operated again until the carriage has been inspected by the risk manager or hisher designee and the horse has been certified for service by a veterinarian licensed in the state  safe operation required a unsafe acts by the horsedrawn carriage driver andor passengers are prohibited b the horsedrawn carriage company acknowledges that its drivers property and operations shall be and remain subject at all times to such reasonable regulation by the city as is or may be necessary to protect the interests of the general public  charitable solicitations footnotes  1  cross reference governmental interest in protecting citizens from fraud registration and identification procedure and from undue interference from strangers importuning citizens in their homes after dark and during the early morning hours the city council recognizes that these regulations operate to restrain first amendment rights but determines that such restraints are reasonable and necessary for the protection set forth in this section  hours for soliciting a no person shall solicit by doortodoor or telephone canvass at the place of residence of anyone from whom a solicitation is sought or within diversion program in general a pursuant to ala 197  121490 the city of eufaula alabama may establish a pretrial diversion program b all discretionary powers endowed by common law and provided by statutes and acts of this state or powers or discretion otherwise provided by law for the city shall be retained c the pretrial diversion program shall be under the direct supervision and control of the presiding judge for the municipality pursuant to any rules and regulations established by the city council the municipal judge with approval of the city council and the city prosecutor may program  12114  definitions for the purposes of this act the following terms shall have the following meanings application fee means a onetime administrative fee imposed by the city as a condition precedent to participation in a pretrial diversion program city prosecutor means the prosecutor appointed by the city council or any legal staff employed by the city prosecutor law enforcement as defined in ala 197  418a11 law enforcement officer as defined in ala 197  3625115 whether employed in the state of alabama or elsewhere offender means any person charged with a criminal offense including but not limited to any misdemeanor violation or traffic offense as defined by the alabama 197 which was allegedly committed in the corporate limits or police jurisdiction of the city pretrial diversion program or program means a program that allows the imposition of the city or by a designated agency of certain conditions of behavior and conduct for a specified period of time upon an offender which allow the offender to have his or her charges reduced dismissed without prejudice or otherwise mitigated should all of the conditions be met during the time frame set by the city prosecutor serious physical injury as defined in ala 197  13a1214 supervision fee means any fee other than the application fee imposed by any agency providing supervision of treatment of the offender  12114  participation a an offender may apply to the court for admittance into the pretrial diversion program admittance into the pretrial diversion program is in the sole discretion of the municipal court judge upon receipt of the application and recommendation of the city prosecutor the judge shall determine whether to grant the individual admittance to the program an offender deemed by the municipal judge or the city prosecutor to be a threat to the safety or wellbeing of the community shall not be eligible for the program b an offender charged with any of the following types of offenses shall be ineligible for admittance 1 any offense involving violence or aggression resulting in injury to a law enforcement officer 2 any offense involving eluding or attempting to elude a law enforcement officer 3 any offense involving violence where weapons are used or where children are victims 4 any driving under the influence charge where serious physical injuries are involved 5 any offense wherein the offender is a public official and the charge is related to the capacity of the offender as a public official 6 the person may not hold a commercial driver license cdl issued in any us state and us possession any us territory or any us insular area or has no conviction for which a commercial driver license was required c the city judge may consider an offender for the pretrial diversion program based on any of the following circumstances 1 there is a probability justice will be served if the offender is placed in the program 2 it is determined that the needs of the state city and of the offender can be met program 3 the offender appears to pose no substantial threat to the safety and wellbeing of the community 4 it appears the offender is not likely to be involved in further criminal activity if the offender complies with all conditions imposed pursuant to the program 5 the offender will likely respond to rehabilitative treatment or counseling 6 the need for restitution for the victim from the offender outweighs the interest of the state and city for incarceration of the offender 7 the city judge may waive any of the standards specified in this subsection c if just or special circumstances dictate  12114  requirements a a recommendation by the city prosecutor is required for participation in the pretrial diversion program upon application by an offender for admission into the pretrial diversion program and prior to admission thereto and as a part of the evaluation process of the city prosecutor the city prosecutor may require the offender to furnish information concerning past criminal history education history work record family history medical or psychiatric treatment or care prescribed or received psychological test taken and any other information concerning the offender which the city prosecutor believes has a bearing on the decision whether or not the offender should be admitted to the program b the city prosecutor may require the offender to submit to any type of test or evaluation process or interview the city prosecutor deems appropriate in evaluating the offender for admittance into the program the costs of any test or evaluation shall be paid by the offender or as otherwise agreed to or provided for by this act the offender shall provide the city prosecutor written consent to allow the city prosecutor to receive any educational work medical psychiatric psychological or other records deemed necessary by the city prosecutor for the evaluation process c following the decision of the city judge to admit the offender into the pretrial diversion program but prior to entry the city prosecutor and the offender shall enter into a written agreement stating the conditions of the participation of the offender in the program the agreement shall include but not be limited to all of the following 1 a voluntary waiver of the right of the offender to a speedy trial 2 an agreement to the tolling while in the program of periods of limitations established by statutes or rules of court 3 an agreement to the conditions of the program established by the city prosecutor 4 if there is a victim of the charged crime an agreement to the restitution repayment within a specified period of time and in an amount to be determined by the city prosecutor taking into account circumstances of the offender and the victim 5 a waiver in writing of the right of the offender to a jury trial 6 a truthful and complete statement by the offender as to the involvement of the offender in the offense charged which statement shall be admissible in any criminal trial 7 submission of a written plea of guilty to the offense or offenses charged or agreed upon included offenses together with an agreement as to whether the case is to be dismissed upon successful completion of the program and an agreement if there be any as to the recommended sentence should a sentence be imposed d in addition to those requirements set forth in subsection c of this section or as a condition of continued participation in the program the city prosecutor may require the offender to agree to any of the following terms or conditions 1 to participate in substance abuse treatment 2 to participate in an education setting to include but not limited to k12 college job training trade school ged classes or basic education courses 3 if appropriate to attempt to learn to read and write the english language 4 to financially support his or her children or pay any court ordered child support 5 to refrain from the use of drugs or alcohol or frequenting places where drugs or alcohol are sold or used 6 to not commit any criminal offense 7 to refrain from contact with certain named persons or premises 8 to maintain or seek employment 9 to not leave the state without prior written consent of the city prosecutor or supervision agency or personnel 10 to maintain a residence approved by the city prosecutor or supervising agency or personnel 11 to attend individual group financial chemical addiction family mental health sex offender or anger management counseling 12 to pay all court costs fees fines and worthless checks and obey any other lawful court order associated with the offense or offenses for which the offender has entered the program or any other case 13 to refrain from the possession or use of any deadly weapon or dangerous instrument as defined in ala 197  13a12 14 to pay supervision fees and application fees pursuant to this act 15 to observe curfews or home detention or travel constraints as set out in agreement signed by the offender 16 to have restitution court costs fees child support and any other moneys withheld or garnished from the wages or salary of the offender or withheld from any alabama income tax due the offender or from any available insurance policy or forfeited from any other real or personal property of the offender and applied to the above 17 to be admitted to a drug or alcohol treatment program on an inpatient or outpatient basis or receive other treatment alternatives for substance abuse 18 to submit to periodic or random drug testing as part of the program and other terms and conditions related to substance abuse as the city prosecutor may direct 19 to waive in writing the right of the offender to a probation hearing in the event of termination or withdrawal from the program 20 to any other terms or conditions as the city prosecutor or his or her designee and the offender may agree to in the abovestated agreement it being the purpose of this act to allow the city prosecutor broad discretion in designing a program specifically for each offender and his or her particular circumstances 21 when applicable to be required to pay supervision fees to the agency or entity responsible for monitoring and verifying the compliance of the offender with the terms of the program set forth by the city prosecutor the fees shall be paid by the offender to the supervising entity in a timely manner 22 community service with an approved community service charitable or nonprofit organization the prosecutor shall compile a list of approved organizations for each participant participants who wish to complete this requirement with an organization not on the prosecutors list must have any such organization preapproved by the prosecutor  12114  fees a an offender may be assessed a nonrefundable application fee when the offender is approved for the pretrial diversion program the amount of the assessment for participation in the program shall be in addition to any court costs fees and assessments for the crime victims compensation fund department of forensic sciences assessments drug alcohol or anger management treatment required by law and any costs of supervision treatment and restitution for which the offender may be responsible the offender will be assessed a $700 fee for the creation maintenance and administration of the pretrial diversion database which shall be remitted to the office of prosecution services in montgomery alabama within 30 days of entry of the offender into the pretrial diversion program a schedule of payments for any of these fees may be established by the city prosecutor b the following maximum applications fees shall be applied to offenders accepted in the program 1 driving under the influence offenses dui up to $250000  2 domestic violence offenses up to $100000  3 other misdemeanor offenses up to $50000  4 traffic offenses not including dui up to $35000  5 violations up to $10000 c the amount of the application fee for each offender shall be established by the city prosecutor and approved by the municipal court judge d all fees assessed and collected by the pretrial diversion program shall be allocated to the general fund of the city to defray the administration costs of the program and for use for any other municipal purpose e an applicant offender may not be denied access into the pretrial diversion program based solely on the inability of the offender to pay the application fee application fees may be reduced but not waived for just cause including indigency of the offender at the discretion of the city any determination of the indigency of the offender for purposes of program fee mitigation shall be made by the city but such mitigation shall be done only upon the determination by the city that there is no reasonable likelihood within the reasonably foreseeable future that the offender will have the ability to pay the application fee f application fees required by this act shall be collected by the court clerk of the city municipal court  12114  approval of the court a upon acceptance of an offender into the pretrial diversion program by the city prosecutor the city prosecutor and the offender shall submit the written application of the offender together with the statement of facts of the offender the acceptance of the offender by the city prosecutor and the agreement between the city prosecutor and the offender to the court presiding over the affected case of the offender for the approval of the court the offender shall also enter a plea of guilty to the charge or charges involved if the court rejects the agreement and guilty plea any money paid by the offender in satisfaction of the application fee shall be refunded to the offender the offender shall still be liable for any actual expenses already incurred by the city prosecutor or any agency or service provider in furtherance of the application and evaluation process and the same will be deducted from any money so refunded to the offender b upon approval of the agreement and acceptance of the guilty plea the court shall expressly retain jurisdiction of the case any other provision of law notwithstanding any may withdraw and file the case or otherwise place it on an administrative docket until such time as the court has been notified that the offender has fulfilled the terms of the agreement has been terminated from the program or otherwise withdrawn from the program imposition of punishment by the court shall be deferred until the offender has successfully completed the program or is terminated from the program c in the event the offender is terminated from the program the court shall impose appropriate punishment in the same manner as with any plea of guilty or finding of guilty and shall not be bound by the terms of agreement as to what punishment to impose d upon successful completion of the program by the offender the city prosecutor shall notify the court in writing of that fact together with a request that the court enter an order of disposition of the case pursuant to the agreement between the offender and the city prosecutor e regardless of whether the offender successfully completes the program or withdraws from or is terminated from the program the offender will still be liable for and required to pay any and all court costs and fees restitution victims compensation fund assessment and any and all other fees and assessments in the same manner as if the offender had not applied for entry into the program and had been found guilty of the offense or offense involved no costs fees restitution or assessments shall be waived or remitted absent an express agreement to that effect between the city prosecutor and the offender without a finding by the court that the offender does not have the reasonable ability to pay the same within the reasonably foreseeable future  12114  violations a after any violation of any program terms or conditions or upon any breach of any program agreement by the offender the city prosecutor may do any of the following 1 continue the agreement with or without modification 2 terminate the offender from the pretrial diversion program 3 require the offender to adopt a new agreement as a condition of continued participation b the city prosecutor may waive a violation for good cause shown why the offender should stay in the program  12114  liability a the city or its officers or employees shall have no liability criminal or civil pursuant to this article the city prosecutor may require written agreed upon waivers of liability as a prerequisite for admittance into the pretrial diversion program f absent wantonness gross
