this article shall not apply to those streets within the city maintained by the state highway department and no person shall excavate cut into take up or undermine such streets without first securing permission from the state highway department  permit required no person shall excavate cut into take up or undermine any street sidewalk alley or other public property without first having obtained a permit from the city clerktreasurer a separate permit must be obtained for the work done on each block or street it shall be the duty of the city clerktreasurer to issue permits to any person who files with him an application and complies with section 8229  cash deposit a to ensure the proper replacing repairing and repaving of any street sidewalk or alley in the city each person making any excavation alteration or cutting into any paved street sidewalk alley or other public property or each person taking up any paving or undermining the street sidewalk alley or other public place in the city shall prior to undertaking to excavate alter or cut the street obtain a permit from the building official who shall require a minimum cash deposit with the city clerktreasurer of $25000 for each such 12 linear foot excavation which portion of the deposit shall be used by the city for the purpose of properly repaving such excavation b the applicant shall be responsible for properly backfilling such excavation with approved material and concrete as provided for in this article c should the sums required in subsection a of this section in the opinion of the building official be insufficient to put the street sidewalk alley or public property back in the same condition the building official shall have the right and authority to require a larger deposit than is required in subsection a of this section as a condition to the building official issuing a permit d the applicant will be refunded onehalf of the deposit when the work is complete and a satisfactory inspection report given by the building official e if the excavation is more than the minimum 12 linear feet an additional $1500 for each additional linear foot will be added to the minimum deposit of $25000 with half of total deposit amount refunded to the applicant upon completion of the work and satisfactory report issued by the building official if the applicant fails to satisfactorily perform the required work within five working days of making the cut weather permitting he shall forfeit the entire deposit  specifications a the applicant for an excavation permit will be required to follow the specifications set out in this section for the backfilling of trenches b the space around the pipe shall be filled with approved backfill material free of stones the material shall be carried up to a point of not less than 12 inches above the top of the pipe approved backfill is to be placed by hand in sixinch layers and tamped around the pipe with a jumping jack or by an alternate method approved by the building official care being taken not to damage or dislocate the pipe this procedure shall continue until the backfill is at least 512 inches from the grade surface four inches of concrete will then be placed on top of the compacted backfill material to be within 112 inches of grade surface the applicant will be required to notify the building official for an inspection of the compacted trench before proceeding with four inches of concrete  secs 82318250  reserved article iii  public assemblies footnotes  2  cross reference offenses against public peace order and safety  66321 et seq division 1  generally definitions the following words terms and phrases when used in this article shall have the meanings ascribed to them in this section except where the context clearly indicates a different meaning church means any building or place of assembly used as a house of worship by any group or congregation of persons of whatever name or calling whether jewish roman catholic greek orthodox unitarian protestant or other epithet means any adjective term phrase or expression which denotes or connotes a quality or attribute regarded as characteristic of a person insulting or fighting words means those words which by their very utterance inflict injury or tend to incite an immediate breach of the peace by the addressee including classical fighting words words in current use less classical but equally likely to cause violence and other disorderly words including profanity obscenity and threats lewd means obscene lustful indecent lascivious lecherous or immoral near means within sight or hearing but in any event shall not include a distance of more than 200 yards obscene means that which is offensive to chastity of mind or to modesty expressing or presenting to the mind or view something that delicacy purity and decency forbids to be exposed it shall also mean that which is indecent lewd licentious foul filthy libidinous and of such character as to deprave and corrupt those whose minds are open to such immoral influences or calculated with the ordinary person to deprave his morals or to lead to impure purposes and tending to excite feelings of an impure or unchaste character stirring the sex impulses and leading to sexually impure and lustful thoughts public assembly refers to any parade march formation procession picket group of pickets picket line demonstration movement assemblage muster or display of persons animals floats motor vehicles or combinations thereof on the public sidewalks streets highways or other public ways for the purpose of 1 presenting a cause  2 expressing an opinion to the general public on any particular issue  3 protesting or influencing any state of affairs or decision rendered or to be rendered thereon whether political economic or social  or 4 celebrating marking or commemorating any past present or future event or occurrence whether historical or otherwise  notwithstanding that such public assembly may be tranquil and devoid of noise tumult and quarrelsome demeanor and does not disturb the public peace and regardless of whether the persons participating and engaging therein march move about or patrol display signs placards flags banners cards or combinations thereof or sing shout chant cant yell or clap their hands  provided however that a funeral procession and service shall not be considered a public assembly residential district means any portion or part of the city that has been designated as a residential district under the zoning ordinance of the city  cross reference definitions and rules of construction generally  12 penalty whoever shall be guilty of any violation of this article shall upon conviction be punished as provided in section 16  purpose the purpose of this article is to 1 promote the public convenience and control travel on the sidewalks streets highways and other public ways in the city by regulating the time place duration and manner of use thereof for public assemblies  2 provide for the concomitant right of free speech and assembly  3 safeguard practical and effective means whereby citizens may express opinions and enlighten the public on the nature and costs of matters of public concern and may petition for redress of grievances  4 vest appropriate and limited regulatory power concerning such in the mayor  and 5 provide for punishment for violations of this article  provisions deemed cumulative the sections provisions and violations of this article are cumulative and in addition to other provisions and violations of other provisions of this ordinances of the city or of the common law or statutes of the state  offenses while participating engaged in or observing public assembly whoever while participating or engaging in or observing a public assembly does any of the following shall on conviction be deemed guilty of an offense 1 addresses any lewd obscene profane libelous insulting or fighting word or words to another  2 disobeys or disregards any traffic control device signal or regulation except when ordered to do so by an officer of the police department  3 utters any abusive epithet toward any person  4 willfully and intentionally urinates or defecates on any sidewalk street highway or public way  5 encourages by word or act or both the commission of any crime or quasicrime  6 assists attempts or participates in cordoning off a sidewalk street highway or other public way or entrance to any building public or private denying thereby free access  7 participates or engages in any illicit sex act  8 willfully and intentionally lies prone or sits upon any sidewalk street highway or other public way so as to obstruct impede hinder stifle retard or restrain passage or traffic thereon  9 assaults spits on or at or throws any missile at any officer of the police department any other law enforcement officer or any person summoned to assist any such officer  or 10 fails or refuses to disperse quickly and quietly at the permitted time  public assemblies in residential district areas the mayor shall refuse to issue a permit for any public assembly in any residential district area it shall be a violation for any person to participate or engage in any public assembly in any such area  encouraging minors to participate it shall be unlawful for any person to aid abet command counsel or induce any minor to participate or engage in any public assembly whether or not such public assembly shall be permitted or not permitted as provided by this article unless prior to the participation or engagement of such minor in such public assembly the consent of the parent or legal guardian of such person shall have been obtained if such participation or engagement occurs during a time at which such person would be required by law to be attending school the prior consent of the principal of the school in which such person is enrolled or if such person is not enrolled in school the superintendent of the school system in which such person would be enrolled shall have first been obtained  action upon assembly becoming violent  failure to disburse on order a upon any public assembly becoming violent any law enforcement officer of the city county or state or any magistrate having jurisdiction within the city or the police jurisdiction thereof may audibly call to a halt such public assembly declare the assembly to have become violent and order those participating therein to disperse b it shall be unlawful for any person having been so ordered to willfully fail or refuse to disperse quickly and quietly c whenever any public assembly shall have become unreasonably loud or boisterous or whenever any brick bottle or other missile shall have been thrown from within the ranks of any public assembly or when the members or participants in any public assembly shall engage in fights or other affrays it shall be presumed that such public assembly has become violent  secs 82598270  reserved division 2  permit required it shall be unlawful for any person to participate or engage in or to aid abet command counsel or induce any person to participate or engage in a public assembly in the city or in the police jurisdiction thereof without there having first been obtained prior thereto a permit for such public assembly  issuance the mayor shall issue a permit required by this division in writing to any person organized group partnership unincorporated association of persons or to any corporation organized and existing under the laws of the state or of any other state provided such corporation is qualified to do business within the state upon proper application therefor the permit shall permit participation and engagement in a public assembly within the city on the terms and conditions and pursuant to the procedure declared in this division  application the application for public assembly permit shall contain the following items of information 1 the name address and telephone number of the person seeking to conduct such public assembly 2 if the public assembly is proposed to be conducted for on behalf of or by an organization the name address and telephone number of the headquarters of the organization and of the authorized and responsible heads of such organization 3 the name address and telephone number of the person who will be the public assembly chairman and who will be responsible for its conduct 4 the date when the public assembly is to be conducted 5 the route to be traveled the starting point and the termination point 6 the approximate number of persons who and animals and vehicles which will constitute such public assembly the type of animals and description of the vehicles 7 the hours when such public assembly will start and terminate 8 a statement as to what portion of the public streets the public assembly will occupy 9 the location by streets of any assembly areas for such public assembly 10 the time at which units of the public assembly will begin to assemble at any such areas 11 the interval of space to be maintained between units of such public assembly 12 if the public assembly is designed to be held by and on behalf of or for any person other than the applicant the applicant for such permit shall file with the mayor a communication in writing from the person proposing to hold the public assembly authorizing the applicant to apply for the permit on his behalf 13 any additional information which the mayor shall find reasonably necessary to a fair determination as to whether a permit should issue  execution of application the application for a permit required by this division must be executed in the name of the organized group partnership unincorporated association of persons or corporation by a person having the authority of a general agent thereof and such execution shall constitute a representation by the person so executing the application that he has such authority the execution of such application by a person who has not such authority shall be deemed a violation and shall be punishable as provided in section 16  contents  violation of conditions prohibited a the permit required by this division shall contain terms and conditions in substantial conformity with the items of information in the application and the mayor or other person acting for him shall modify where possible any item of information which left unmodified would necessitate the refusal of the permit no other term or condition shall be placed in the permit except such as is reasonably necessary for the safety and protection of those engaging or participating in such public assembly for the maintenance of adequate police fire and ambulance protection throughout the municipality and for the reasonable convenience of the public use of the public sidewalks streets highways and other ways b it shall be a violation for any person participating or engaging in such public assembly to disregard or fail or refuse to obey any term or condition in the permit and it shall further be the duty of every person engaging in a public assembly to ascertain the terms and conditions of the permit allowing such assembly  delivery of application  permit deemed granted if not acted upon every application for a permit required by this division shall manually be delivered to the city clerktreasurer or to his designated representative in the office of the city clerktreasurer by the person executing the application the person delivering such application shall upon demand be given a written receipt for the application identifying it and showing its time of delivery the person executing and delivering such application and no other shall appear at the office of the city clerktreasurer not less than six days after delivering the application and not less than 48 hours prior to the requested commencement of such public assembly and then and there request the permit applied for if at the time of such request no action shall have been taken either granting or denying the permit the permit shall be considered to have been granted  location near churches the mayor shall refuse to issue a permit for any public assembly at or near any church unless the local governing body of the church shall consent in writing to the issuance of the permit however nothing contained in this section shall be construed to prohibit the normal religious services at any church nor any meeting of all or part of the membership of any such church and persons invited by members of such church from meeting at such church or upon the grounds of such church nothing contained in this section shall prohibit a parade or other public assembly from merely passing by at or near any church so long as such passing by is not for the purpose of disturbing a worship service at such church  refusal the mayor shall refuse to issue a permit for a public assembly unless each of the following conditions is apparent from clear and convincing evidence or is evident from the application itself 1 the conduct of the public assembly will not substantially interrupt the safe and orderly movement of other traffic contiguous to its route 2 the conduct of the public assembly will not require the diversion of so great a number of police officers of the city properly to police the line of movement and the areas contiguous thereto as to prevent normal police protection to the city 3 the conduct of such public assembly will not require the diversion of so great a number of ambulances as to prevent normal ambulance service to portions of the city other than that to be occupied by the proposed line of march and areas contiguous thereto 4 the concentration of persons animals and vehicles at assembly points of the public assembly will not unduly interfere with proper fire and police protection of or ambulance service to areas contiguous to such assembly areas 5 the conduct of such public assembly will not interfere with the movement of firefighting equipment enroute to a fire 6 the conduct of the public assembly is not reasonably likely to cause injury to persons or property to provoke disorderly conduct or create a disturbance 7 the public assembly is scheduled to move from its point of origin to its point of termination expeditiously and without unreasonable delays en route 8 the public assembly is not to be held for the sole purpose of advertising any product goods or event and is not designed to be held purely for private profit  taxation footnotes  1  cross reference finance  2291 included in the monthly statement required by section 86741 or with the other information requested pursuant to section 86742 of this division d the failure to pay the amount of tax due under this division on the date the same is due any act or omission declared above to be a violation of this division shall be a continuing offense or violation of this division and each day during which such act or omission continues shall constitute a separate offense any person who commits an act or omission declared above to be a violation of this division shall upon conviction be punished by a fine of designated truck routes city  signs the chief of police shall cause to be erected and maintained at points where routes enter the city at all junctions points and turns where necessary such signs and such directions at such locations as shall be approved by the chief of police directing truck traffic in accordance with the provisions of this division  trucks not on designated routes any truck violating this division however nothing in this section would prevent the driver from producing other type of evidence that he has a load of goods wares or merchandise on his truck consigned to a business in the city  special requirements for trucks and buses with more than two axles and all tractortrailers a trucks and buses with more than two axles and all tractortrailers shall use the right handicapped parking footnotes  4  editors note adopted  repealed ch 90 art iv div 2  9017190176 in its entirety subsequently said ordinance added  9017190180 to read as herein set out formerly said division pertained to similar subject matter and derived from 78 handicapped individual defined for the purposes of this article the term handicapped individual shall mean any person who has a permanent or temporary for a period up to one year physical impairment or permanent mental impairment which limits mobility to the extent that the individual would have difficulty safely walking alone or walking without physical pain a distance of 50 feet or more  distinctive decal authorized  required  medical proof etc any person who submits to the judge of probate medical proof satisfactory to said issuing authority that he or she is a disabled individual as herein defined shall be issued either a distinctive license plate or a decal and a special identification placard displaying the international system of access thereby designating the driver of the vehicle or the passenger as being a disabled person the distinctive license plate decals and placards provided herein shall be prepared by the judge of probate and shall be issued in the same manner as motor vehicle license plates  unlimited parking periods exceptions the disabled individual to whom valid distinctive license plates andor decals or placards are issued shall be allowed to park for unlimited periods in parking zones designated for disabled persons provided however that such disabled persons shall pay parking fees the same as any other person the provisions of this section shall not apply to zones where stopping standing or parking is prohibited to all vehicles or zones which are reserved for special types of vehicles nor will these provisions apply where there is a local ordinance prohibiting parking during heavy traffic periods during morning afternoon or evening rush hours or where parking would clearly present a traffic hazard in designated disabled loading zones disabled persons shall be limited to one hour parking as these loading zones are not intended for unlimited parking usage  false representation or misuse of parking privileges unlawful it shall be unlawful for any person who is not a disabled individual as herein defined to willfully and falsely represent himself or herself as a disabled person to obtain the distinctive license plate andor decal or placard or to misuse or abuse the parking privilege protected by this division or to own a vehicle bearing distinctive license plate andor decals when not entitled to do so under the provisions of this division or to park an automobile having a handicapped tag or decal or to use a handicap placard unless the person to whom said handicapped license plate decal or special identification placard is issued is physically present in the automobile at the time said automobile is actually parked in any zone designated for handicap only or disabled only parking  unauthorized use unlawful a it shall be unlawful for any person to park any vehicle in any zone designated for handicap only or disabled only parking not bearing the distinctive license plate andor decal or placard or to park any vehicle in violation of any part of this division or in violation of any state statute it shall also be unlawful for any person to park any vehicle or to allow the placement of any material or other equipment which would block an access ramp or curb cut b it shall be unlawful for any person who does not have a distinctive handicapped decal or placard or temporarily handicapped placard as provided for in section 90172 to park a motor vehicle in a parking place designated for the handicapped at any place of public accommodation amusement or resort or any other place to which the general public in invited even though located on private property and upon conviction thereof shall be fined as hereinafter provided c any authorized municipal county or state law enforcement officer may go onto private property to enforce the provisions of this section d the provisions of this section shall be held in pari materia with all other provisions of law related to illegal handicapped parking violations  provided however that all municipal laws or parts of municipal laws which conflict with the provision of this section are hereby repealed  parking spaces designated the police chief is authorized to designate marked parking spaces for the exclusive parking of motor vehicles of handicapped individuals or temporarily handicapped individuals as defined by ala 197  revocation or cancellation of authorization for use of decals and placards the use of any decals or placards for parking in handicapped spaces within the city may be revoked or cancelled for abuse misuse or unauthorized use by persons other than the authorized handicapped individual in such event the revoked or cancelled permit shall not be valid in the city  handicapped spaces on private property with the consent of the property owner the police chief is authorized to designate certain parking spaces in privately owned parking areas to be posted as parking for the handicapped under the provisions of this division and subject to the same regulations the cost of the sign and installation by the city shall be paid to the city by the owner prior to delivery or installation of any such sign  penalties for unlawful acts any person committing any act declared to be unlawful by this division shall be guilty of an offense against the city and shall upon conviction be punished as follows 1st offense $5000 2nd offense 10000 3rd offense 50000 plus applicable court costs in addition any automobile unlawfully occupying a parking zone designated for disabled or handicapped persons may be towed away at the owners expense such fines shall be paid in the same manner as other municipal fines for driving violations except section 16  abandonment prohibited  presumption of abandonment no person shall abandon any vehicle within the city or its police jurisdiction it shall be presumed that any vehicle that has been left at any place on a street or highway within the city or its police jurisdiction for a period of 72 hours consecutively is an abandoned vehicle  leaving wrecked nonoperating vehicle on street no person shall leave any partially dismantled nonoperating wrecked or junked vehicle on any street or highway within the city or its police jurisdiction  discarded wrecked or junked vehicles on private property no person in charge or control of any property within the city or its police jurisdiction whether as owner tenant occupant lessee or otherwise shall allow any partially dismantled nonoperating wrecked junked or discarded vehicle to remain on such property longer than 72 hours no person shall leave any such vehicle on any property within the city or its police jurisdiction for a longer time than 72 hours however this section shall not apply to a vehicle in an enclosed building a vehicle on the premises of a business enterprise operated in a lawful place and manner when necessary to the operation of such business enterprise or a vehicle in an appropriate storage place or depository maintained in a lawful place and manner by the city  removal or impoundment of vehicles the chief of police or any member of his department designated by him is authorized to remove or have removed any vehicle left at any place within the city or its police jurisdiction which reasonably appears to be in violation of this article or to be a lost stolen or unclaimed vehicle any vehicle so taken up and removed shall be stored in a suitable place provided by the city to protect it from deterioration a permanent record giving the date of the taking of each vehicle the place where found and taken and a description of the vehicle shall be kept by the chief of police  public sale of impounded vehicles at least every six months the chief of police shall sell at public auction to the highest bidder for cash the vehicles authorized in this article to be removed and taken up and which shall have been taken up and stored for a period of three months or more the sales shall be made after notice of the time and place therefor shall have first been given by publication once a week for two successive weeks in a newspaper of general circulation published in the city the first publication shall be at least 20 days before the sale each vehicle shall be sold separately and a notation in the storage record book shall be made of the amount received for each vehicle the person making the sale shall have the right to reject any and all bids if the amount bid is unreasonably low and shall have the right to continue the sales from time to time if no bidders are present after deducting and paying all expenses incurred in the removal taking up storing maintaining and selling of the vehicle the balance if any shall be paid into the general fund of the city  redemption of impounded vehicles prior to sale the owner of any vehicle taken up and stored as provided in this article may redeem the vehicle at any time prior to its sale by paying the reasonable expense of taking the vehicle in charge its maintenance and storage and a pro rata amount of connection of residences to public water system it shall be unlawful for any person to reside in any residence or building designed for occupancy or used as a singlefamily residence unless such building or residence is connected to and supplied with water from the public water system in the city by the mains or pipes of the public water system in the city it shall be unlawful for any person to let or rent any such residence or building unless the residence or building is so connected and supplied however this section shall not apply when the lot or parcel of land upon which the residence or building is situated is more than 100 feet from the nearest water supply main or pipe located within a public way or rightofway which abuts or adjoins such lot or parcel of land upon which is situated the residence or building  connection of apartments to public water supply it shall be unlawful for any person to reside in any apartment in any building which is designed for occupancy or used as a singlefamily residence unless such apartment is connected to and supplied with water from the public water system in the city by the mains or pipes of the public water system in the city it shall be unlawful for any owner agent or person to let or rent any such apartment in any apartment building unless the apartment is so connected and supplied  use of wells and springs it shall be unlawful to construct maintain use or permit to be used any spring well cistern or other excavation as a source of domestic water supply for any dwelling building or premises located within 100 feet of the water main or pipe as provided in section 9417  unauthorized extension of service it shall be unlawful for any person in any manner whatever to extend or alter any service or other pipe or attachment of any kind connecting or water from the public water system in the city is furnished from the water mains or pipes or source of supply  use of water from fire hydrant it shall be unlawful for any person to take carry away or use any water from the public water system in the city from a fire hydrant or fireplug in a public way except for use in fighting fire without authority from the waterworks and sewer board  obstructing fire hydrants and stopcocks it shall be unlawful for any person to obstruct access to any fire hydrant stopcock or other fixture connected with the supply of water from the public water system in the city by placing thereon stone brick lumber dirt or any other material or to permit any other material to be placed thereon by those in his employ  fire hydrants for use of fire department the fire hydrants are for the use of the fire department and for the extinguishment of fires and must be used by firefighters only and for no other purpose except upon written permission of an official or employee of the waterworks and sewer board acting in accordance with regulations of the waterworks and sewer board  tapping mains or cutting off water it shall be unlawful for any person except an official or employee of the waterworks and sewer board acting in accordance with regulations of such board to tap any main forming a part of the public water system in the city or to connect any service pipe therewith or to turn on or shut off water from the main except in case of accident or emergency  use after shutoff it shall be unlawful for any person to cause or suffer any premises of which he is in charge or control to be supplied with water from the public water system in the city after such water has been rightfully shut off  turning on water after shutoff it shall be unlawful for any person other than an authorized officer of the waterworks and sewer board or employee of the board in the course of his duty to turn on water from the public water system in the city after the water has been turned off by the authorized agents of the waterworks and sewer board  use without metering a it shall be unlawful for any person to connect a tub pipe other instrument or contrivance to any pipe used for supplying water from the public water system in the city or in any manner to change alter extend connect or disconnect any pipe meter or attachment by which the water is or is about to be furnished or supplied in such manner that any water from the public water system in the city is or can be used or consumed without passing properly registering upon the meter or other measuring instrument provided for registering the quantity used or consumed b it shall be unlawful for any person to turn on the flow of water from the public water system in the city of the pipes or mains of the public water system in the city with the intent or purpose of obtaining the use of such water without paying for the water  interference with equipment it shall be unlawful for any person to in any manner destroy alter impair or prevent the proper action of any meter or other instrument used to measure the consumption of water from the public water system in the city or to connect disconnect reconnect or in any manner interfere with damage or destroy any main pipe meter valve stopcock or other appliance machinery or equipment of the public water system in the city  diversion of water from system it shall be unlawful for any person having charge or control of any pipe supplied with water from the public water system by the public water system to allow or permit any person to take draw or use any water therefrom prior to the time of passage of such water meter used for measuring consumption  evidence of violations proof that any of the acts specified in this article were done or permitted on the premises in charge of the accused or that the accused received the benefit of any of such acts shall be prima facie evidence that the accused committed aided or abetted in the commission of such acts  contamination of water supply it shall be unlawful for any person to in any way defile or contaminate or attempt to defile or contaminate the water from the public water system in the city in any reservoir pipe main public fountain or stream connected with the approved public water supply of the waterworks and sewer board  secs 94329450  reserved article iii  sewers and sewage disposal footnotes  3  cross reference plumbing code  18286 et seq  health and sanitation ch 50 state law reference municipal sewers ala 197  115051 division 1  generally definitions the following words terms and phrases when used in this article shall have the meanings ascribed to them in this section except where the context clearly indicates a different meaning board means the waterworks and sewer board of the city bod denoting biochemical oxygen demand means the quantity of oxygen utilized in the biochemical oxidation of organic matter under standard laboratory procedure of five days at 20 degrees celsius expressed in milligrams per liter building drain means that part of the lowest horizontal piping of a drainage system which receives the discharge from soil waste and other drainage pipes inside the walls of the building and conveys it to the building sewer beginning five feet 15 meters outside the outer face of the building wall building sewer means the extension from the building drain to the public sewer or other place of disposal cfr is an abbreviation for federal regulations combined sewer means a sewer receiving both surface runoff and sewage garbage means solid wastes from the domestic and commercial preparation cooking and dispensing of food and from the handling storage and sale of produce industrial wastes means the liquid wastes from industrial manufacturing processes trade or business as distinct from sanitary sewage natural outlet means any outlet into a watercourse pond ditch lake or other body of surface water or groundwater osha is an abbreviation for occupational safety and health administration ph means the logarithm of the reciprocal of the weight of hydrogen ions in grams per liter of solution properly shredded garbage means the wastes from the preparation cooking and dispensing of food that have been shredded to such a degree that all particles will be carried freely under the flow conditions normally prevailing in public sewers with no particle greater than onehalf inch 127 centimeters in any dimension public sewer means a sewer in which all owners of abutting properties have equal rights and which is controlled by public authority sanitary sewer means a sewer which carries sewage and to which stormwater surface water and groundwater are not intentionally admitted sewage means a combination of the watercarried wastes from residences business buildings institutions and industrial establishments together with such groundwaters surface waters and stormwaters as may be present sewage treatment plant means any arrangement of devices and structures used for treating sewage sewer means a pipe or conduit for carrying sewage sewer works means all facilities for collecting pumping treating and disposing of sewage slug means any discharge of water sewage or industrial waste which in concentration of any given constituent or in quantity of flow exceeds for any period of duration longer than 15 minutes more than five times the average 24hour concentration or flow during normal operation storm drain or storm sewer means a sewer which carries stormwaters and surface waters and drainage but excludes sewage and industrial wastes other than unpolluted cooling water superintendent means the general manager of the waterworks and sewer board or his authorized deputy agent or representative or the boards engineer while superintendent can also be the boards engineer the boards engineer does not mean the superintendent suspended solids means solids that are in suspension in water sewage or other liquids and which are removable by laboratory filtering water board means the waterworks and sewer board watercourse means a channel in which a flow of water occurs either continuously or intermittently art i 112190 cross reference definitions and rules of construction generally  12 violations a any person found to be violating any provision of this article shall be served by the board with written notice stating the nature of the violation and providing a reasonable time limit for the satisfactory correction thereof the offender shall within the period of time stated in such notice permanently cease all violations b any person who shall continue any violation beyond the time limit provided for in subsection a of this section shall be guilty of a misdemeanor and upon conviction thereof shall be punished as provided in section 16 c any person violating any of the provisions of this article shall become liable to the waterworks and sewer facilities should be issued when approved and periodic inspections should be made by the plumbing inspector or the local health department depending on who issues the permits art iii 112190 right of entry a the superintendent and other duly authorized employees of the board bearing proper credentials and identification shall be permitted to enter all properties for the purposes of inspection observation measurement sampling and testing in accordance with the provisions of this article the superintendent or his representatives shall have no authority to inquire into any processes including metallurgical chemical oil refining ceramic paper or other industries beyond that point having a direct bearing on the kind and source of discharge to the sewers or waterways or facilities for waste treatment b while performing the necessary work on private properties referred to in subsection a of this section the superintendent or duly authorized employees of the board shall observe all safety rules applicable to the premises established by the company and the company shall be held harmless for injury or death to the board employees the board shall indemnify the company against loss or damage to its property by board employees and against liability claims and demands for personal injury or property damage asserted against the company and growing out of the gauging and sampling operation except as such may be caused by negligence or failure of the company to maintain safe conditions as required in section 9498 c the superintendent and other duly authorized employees of the board bearing proper credentials and identification shall be permitted to enter all private properties the board holds a duly negotiated easement for the purposes of but not limited to inspection observation measurement sampling repair and maintenance of any portion of the sewer works lying within the easement all entry and subsequent work if any on the easement shall be done in full accordance with the terms of the duly negotiated easement pertaining to the private property involved art vii 112190   secs 94569465  reserved division 2  building sewers and connections permit a no building at an elevation below the basement floor in all buildings in which any building drain is too low to permit gravity flow to the public sewer sanitary sewage carried by such building drain shall be lifted by an approved means and discharged to the building sewer c the connection of the building sewer into the public sewer shall conform to the requirements of the building and plumbing codes or other applicable rules and regulations of the city or the procedures set forth in appropriate specifications of the astm and wpcf manual of practice no 9 all such connections shall be made gastight and watertight any deviation from the prescribed procedures and materials must be approved by the superintendent before installation d except in cases where the superintendent shall otherwise approve in writing as a permit condition all connections to existing sewers shall be made by employees of the board the connecting building sewers installed by the board shall include tap or wye and sufficient building service line to extend the building sewer to at least three feet beyond the streets traveled way pavement curb or sidewalk on the side of those facilities nearest the proposed building to be served at that point the board will install a plug pending extension of the building sewer by the permittee the board shall charge a fee for its costs in making the sewer connection and building sewer extension the fee shall be payable when the permit is obtained e building sewers shall be of pvc sdr 35 or stiffer extra strength vc castductile iron or cisp and shall have a minimum diameter of four inches building sewers with less than two feet of cover shall be iron larger diameter pipe may be required by the superintendent if estimated flows so indicate minimum building sewer or rubber shall be used cleanouts shall be subject to approval by the superintendent cleanouts shall be placed a minimum of 75 feet apart with one being located at the property line or at the point of outlet approved by the state department of environmental management or the us environmental protection agency industrial cooling water or unpolluted process waters may be discharged on approval of the state department of environmental management or the environmental protection agency to a storm sewer or natural outlet art v  2 112190 prohibited discharges no person shall discharge or cause to be discharged any of the following described waters or wastes to any public sewers 1 any gasoline benzene naphtha fuel oil or other flammable or explosive liquid solid or gas 2 any waters or wastes containing toxic poisonous solids liquids or gases in sufficient quantity either singly or by interaction with other wastes to interfere with any sewage treatment process constitute a hazard to humans or animals create a public nuisance or create any hazard in the receiving waters of the sewage treatment plant 3 any waters or wastes having a ph lower than 55 or having any other corrosive property capable of causing damage or hazard to structures equipment and personnel of the sewer works 4 solid or viscous substances in quantities or of such size capable of causing obstruction to the flow in sewers or other interference with the proper operation of the sewer works such as but not limited to ashes cinders sand mud straw shavings metal glass rags feathers tar plastics wood unground garbage whole blood paunch manure hair and fleshings entrails and paper dishes cups milk containers etc either whole or ground by garbage grinders art v  3 112190 discharge of harmful substances no person shall discharge or cause to be discharged the following described substances materials waters or wastes if it appears likely in the opinion of the superintendent that such wastes can harm either the sewers sewage treatment process or equipment have an adverse effect on the receiving stream or can otherwise endanger life limb public property or constitute a nuisance in forming his opinion as to the acceptability of these wastes the superintendent will give consideration of such factors as the quantities of wastes in relation to flows and velocities in the sewers materials of construction of the sewers nature of the sewage treatment process capacity of the sewage treatment plant degree of treatability of wastes in the sewage treatment plant and other pertinent factors the substances prohibited are 1 any liquid or vapor having a temperature higher than 150 degrees fahrenheit 65 degrees celsius 2 any water or waste containing fats wax grease or oils whether emulsified or not in excess of 100 mgl or containing substances which may solidify or become viscous at temperatures between 32 and 150 degrees fahrenheit 0 and 65 degrees celsius 3 any garbage that has not been properly shredded the installation and operation of any garbage grinder equipped with a motor of threefourths horsepower 076 hp metric or greater shall be subject to review and approval of the superintendent 4 any waters or wastes containing strong acid iron pickling wastes or concentrated plating solutions whether neutralized or not 5 any waters or wastes containing iron chromium copper zinc cyanide and similar objectionable or toxic substances or wastes exerting an excessive chlorine requirement to such degree that any such material received in the composite sewage at the sewage treatment works exceeds the limits established by the superintendent or the state department of environmental management or the us environmental protection agency for such materials 6 any waters or wastes containing phenols or other taste or odorproducing substances in such concentrations exceeding limits which may be established by the superintendent as necessary after treatment of the composite sewage to meet the requirements of the state federal or other public agencies of jurisdiction for such discharge to the receiving waters 7 any radioactive wastes or isotopes of such halflife or concentration as may exceed limits established by the superintendent in compliance with applicable state or federal regulations 8 any waters or wastes having a ph in excess of 95 9 materials which exert or cause a unusual concentrations of inert suspended solids such as but not limited to fullers earth lime slurries and lime residues or of dissolved solids such as but not limited to sodium chloride and sodium sulfate b excessive discoloration such as but not limited to dye wastes and vegetable tanning solutions c unusual bod above 270 mgl chemical oxygen demand or chlorine requirement in such quantities as to constitute a significant load on the sewage treatment works d unusual volume of flow or concentration of wastes constituting slugs 10 waters or wastes containing substances which are not amenable to treatment or reduction by the sewage treatment processes employed or are amenable to treatment only to such degree that the sewage treatment plant effluent cannot meet the requirements of other agencies having jurisdiction over discharge to the receiving waters 11 waters or wastes containing suspended solids in excess of 320 mgl art v  4 112190 authority over prohibited wastes a if any waters or wastes are discharged or are proposed to be discharged to the public sewers which waters contain the substances or possess the characteristics enumerated in section 9494 and which in the judgement of the superintendent or the state department of environmental management or the us environmental protection agency may have a deleterious effect upon the sewer works processes equipment or receiving waters or which otherwise create a hazard to life or constitute a public nuisance the superintendent may 1 reject the wastes  2 require pretreatment to an acceptable condition for discharge to the public sewers  3 require control over the quantities and rates of discharge  andor 4 require payment to cover the added cost of handling and treating the wastes not covered by existing taxes or sewer charges under the provisions of section 94100 b if the superintendent permits the pretreatment or equalization of waste flows the design and installation of the plants and equipment shall be subject to the review and approval of the boards engineer and the state department of environmental management or the us environmental protection agency and subject to the requirements of all applicable codes ordinances and laws art v  5 112190 interceptors grease oil and sand interceptors shall be provided when in the opinion of the superintendent they are necessary for the proper 112190 maintenance of facilities where preliminary treatment or flowequalizing facilities are provided for any waters or wastes they shall be maintained continuously in satisfactory and effective required shall be accessibly and safely located and shall be constructed in accordance with plans approved by the superintendent the manhole shall be maintained by him to be safe and accessible at all times art v  8 112190 measurements tests and analyses all measurements tests and analyses of the characteristics of waters and wastes to which reference is made in this article shall be determined in accordance with the latest edition of standard methods for the examination of water and wastewater published by the american public health association and shall be determined at the control manhole provided or upon suitable samples taken at the control manhole if no special manhole has been required the control manhole shall be considered to be the nearest downstream manhole in the public sewer to the point at which the building sewer is connected sampling shall be carried out by customarily accepted methods to reflect the effect of constituents upon the sewer works and to determine the existence of hazards to life limb and property the particular analyses involved will determine whether a 24hour composite of all outfalls of a premises is appropriate or whether a grab sample shall be taken normally but not always bod and suspended solids analyses are obtained from 24hour composites of all outfalls whereas phs are determined from periodic grab samples art v  9 112190 special note in order to add the provisions of art ii adopted oct 20 199 to art ii and for purposes of proper classification the existing provisions of art ii consisting of  98169823 have been placed under the title of div 1 abatement of weeds favorable to insects designation of substitute for municipal judge the mayor may designate a city officer or city employee to perform certain functions of the municipal judge under this article  provided however only the municipal judge shall be authorized to conduct hearings involving the issuance of a summons and complaint  removal of weeds or grass favorable to insects a every person owning or having in charge any premises in the city or its police jurisdiction shall keep the premises free of any growth of weeds trash or grass favorable to the harboring of mosquitoes or other insects of like kind every such growth of weeds or grass or accumulation of trash is declared to be a nuisance and every such person who shall allow any such growth of weeds or grass or trash to accumulate on such premises shall be punished as for a violation of this section any criminal action for a violation of the provisions of this article shall be commenced by the issuance of a summons and complaint in lieu of custodial arrest as provided for in section 113 b any growth of weeds or grass more than one foot in height or the accumulation of trash other than in an approved covered receptacle shall be deemed favorable to the harboring of mosquitoes or insects of like kind within the meaning of this article    notice of violation a whenever any official of the city so designated by the mayor to enforce the provisions of this chapter shall discover on any premises in the city or its police jurisdiction any growth of weeds or grass or trash in violation of section 9817 he shall give written notice to the owner or person having such premises in charge to appear before the municipal judge at a time and place to be fixed in the notice and then and there show cause why the growth of weeds or grass or trash should not be declared a nuisance and an order issued requiring the weeds or grass to be cut and removed or the trash to be properly disposed of b the notice shall be in substantially the following form notice to the owner or owners of here describing the property in the city of eufaula you are hereby notified that there exists on the above mentioned property a growth of weeds or grass or accumulation of trash in violation of chapter 98 article ii of the ordinances city of eufaula alabama and you are further notified that a hearing will be conducted by the ____________  ____________  ____________ of the city of eufaula at _____ am on the ____________ day of ____________  ____________  ____________  19 ____________  at which time and place you are directed to appear and show cause if any you can why the existence of said growth of weeds or grass or accumulation of trash should not be declared a nuisance and an order issued requiring the same to be cut and removed or properly disposed of you are hereby further notified that if said growth or trash is not removed within five days after same has been ordered cut andor removed the superintendent of streets or his designees will enter upon said premises and will have the same cut and removed at your cost and expense and will certify the cost and expense to the city council and will ask the city council to assess the said cost against you and the above described property and thereafter the said expense will constitute a lien on said property you are further advised that your failure to comply with this ordinance may result in a summons and complaint being issued commanding you to appear before the municipal court for possible punishment in accordance with the city code dated this ____________ day of ____________  ____________  ____________  19 ____________  _____ c if the mayor has pursuant to section 9816 designated another person to perform the functions of the municipal judge under this article the notice shall reflect the title of such person    service or posting of notice the notice provided for in section 9818 shall be served upon the owner of the property or the person having the property in charge as the case may be if either is known and can be found within the city or its police jurisdiction if such persons are not known or cannot be found within the city or its police jurisdiction service of the notice shall be effected by posting one copy thereof on the premises where the growth of weeds or grass or accumulation of trash is found to exist and the notice shall be served or posted as the case may be at least five days before the date fixed for the hearing    hearing  order to cut or remove weeds or grass or trash at the time and place appointed in the notice provided for in section 9818 the municipal judge or person so designated by the mayor under section 9816 shall conduct a hearing for the purpose of determining whether the growth of weeds or grass or trash complained of exists in violation of this article if he finds that the growth constitutes a violation of this article he shall so declare and shall make an order requiring the cutting and removal of the growth or accumulation of trash of weeds or grass or trash within five days from the making of the order such order shall be served as provided for in section 9819    failure to comply with order the owner or person having in charge any such premises who having been personally served with the notices provided for in section 9818 shall fail to comply with the order of the municipal judge or such person so designated by the mayor under section 9816 requiring the cutting and removal of such weeds or grass or the proper disposal of such trash shall be summoned by summons and complaint to appear before the municipal court and if found guilty of a violation of this section shall be punished as provided in section 16    cutting and removal by city if the owner or person having in charge any premises whereon there exists any growth of weeds or grass or trash in violation of this article shall fail to cut and remove the growth or properly dispose of such trash within five days after the cutting and removal thereof has been ordered by the municipal judge or person so designated by the mayor the superintendent of streets or his designees shall enter upon the premises and at the expense of such person shall proceed to cut and remove the weeds or grass or trash the superintendent of streets is directed to keep an account of the expense of cutting and removing such weeds or grass or trash and to certify the expense monthly to the city council the superintendent of streets shall keep separate accounts showing the total expense of cutting and removing the weeds or grass or trash from each separate lot or premises and to certify the expense to the city council he shall report separately as to each piece of property wherefrom he has cut and removed weeds or grass or trash together with a description of the premises and the name of the owner or persons having the premises in charge thereof if known and the total expense incurred in abating each such nuisance if prisoners are employed in cutting and removing such weeds or grass or trash a reasonable charge for their labors shall be included in the expense to be charged against the property owner or occupant of the premises    hearing and assessments of liens for city charges a at intervals to be determined by the city council it shall cause to be made a list showing the names of the owners or persons who had in charge the premises from which weeds or grass or trash have been removed at the expense of such persons as provided in this article together with a description of the property from which the weeds or grass or trash has been removed and a statement of the amount of the expense as reported by the superintendent of streets of cutting and removing the weeds or grass or trash from each such piece of property if the names of the owners of the property are not known the names may be stated as unknown b the city council shall set a time and place when such persons may appear and show cause if any they can why the expenses should not be assessed against them and their respective premises and shall cause a notice to be published one time in some newspaper published in the city such publication to be made at least ten days in advance of the date fixed for the hearing c at the time and place fixed for the hearing the city council shall proceed to hear and determine any objections that may be interposed to such assessments unless good cause shall be shown against the right of the city to assess the expenses the council shall proceed to levy an assessment against the owners and their respective premises from which weeds or grass or trash have been cut and removed for the expense of cutting and removing such weeds or grass or trash and for all costs incurred in mail and advertising assessment so made shall be final the city shall have a charge and claim against such persons and a lien on the property so assessed for the amount of the respective assessments which lien and charge it shall proceed to enforce and collect as any other debts are collected or liens enforced the cost of recording such assessment shall be added to the assessment together with interest on any unpaid amount so provided by law calculated from the date of assessment    state law reference authority to cut weeds at property owners expense ala 197  1147140 secs 98249830  reserved division 2  abatement of dangerous weeds weeds andor trash may be declared a public nuisance and abated trash is defined in accord with its usual definition to mean something no longer readily useful or not usable in its existing form  something that is tattered worn out broken up or otherwise worthless  rubbish  loppings twigs grass cuttings limbs leaves of trees and similar items of a vegetative nature  refuse trash which has accumulated on private property within the city of eufaula and which is not enclosed in a container and all weeds growing upon streets sidewalks and private property which bear seeds of a wingy or downy nature may be declared to be a public nuisance by the governing body of the city of eufaula and may be abated as hereinafter provided art ii1 102097  art ii1 report of appropriate city official  resolution declaring a public nuisance the term appropriate city official as used in this article shall mean any city official or employee designated by the mayor or other chief executive officer of the city of eufaula as the person to exercise the authority and perform the duties delegated by this article to the appropriate city official the appropriate city official shall report to the city governing body whenever trash has accumulated and weeds are growing upon any street sidewalk or private property which constitute a nuisance upon receiving a report the city governing body may declare the same to be a public nuisance and order its abatement art ii2 102097  art ii2 notice to owner  contents  posting of signs after the passage of a resolution the appropriate city official shall send notice of the action to the last person or persons firm association or corporation last assessing the property for state taxes by certified or registered mail to the address on file in the revenue commissioners office to remedy the growth of weeds and accumulation of trash within a reasonable time set out in the notice not to exceed 14 days or suffer the weeds and trash to be abated by the city and the cost thereof assessed against the property the mailing of the certified or registered notice properly addressed and postage prepaid shall constitute notice as required herein the city shall also place a sign conspicuously on the property indicating that the city governing body has found the property to be a public nuisance because of the unlawful growth of weeds andor accumulation of trash art ii3 102097  art ii3 hearing within the time specified in the notice but not more than fourteen 14 days from the date the notice is given any person firm or corporation may file a written request for a hearing before the governing body of the city together with objections to the finding by the city governing body that the weeds or trash constitute a public nuisance the filing of the request shall hold in abeyance any action on the finding of the city governing body until a determination thereon is made by the city governing body the hearing shall be held not less than five 5 nor more than thirty 30 days after the request in the event that no hearing is timely requested the mayor of the city governing body shall order the weeds andor trash to be abated as hereinafter provided art ii4 102097  art ii4 entry of municipal employees and agents on property to abate nuisance  abatement by private contractor if the nuisance on the property has not been abated within 14 days after the city governing bodys resolution the mayor of the city shall order the nuisance to be abated the abatement may be accomplished at the option of the city by its own forces or by contract for purposes of this article compliance with the competitive bid laws shall not be required all city employees and duly authorized agents are expressly authorized to enter private property for the purpose of abating the nuisance thereon art ii5 102097 accounting of cost of abatement the appropriate city official shall give an itemized written report to the city governing body regarding the cost of abating the nuisance the cost of abatement shall be the actual cost the city incurs in the abatement including administrative costs should the city contract for abatement the cost shall be the actual costs the contractor charges the city for the abatement including administrative costs the city incurs upon report of the costs by the appropriate city official the governing body shall adopt a resolution confirming the costs of the reports provided that any person firm or corporation having an interest in the property may be heard at the meeting concerning the fixing of the costs or the amounts thereof the city clerk of the city shall give at least ten days notice of the meeting at which the fixing of the costs is to be considered by firstclass mail to all entities having an interest in the property whose address and interest is determined from the revenue commissioners records on the property or is otherwise known to the clerk art ii6 102097 cost to constitute weed andor trash liens  report to revenue commissioner  amounts to be included in tax bills  collection the confirmed cost of abatement shall hereinafter be referred to as a weed andor trash lien and thus made and confirmed shall constitute a weed andor trash lien on the property for the amount of the weed andor trash lien after confirmation of the reports a copy shall be turned over to the revenue commissioner of barbour county who under the optional method of taxation is charged with the collection of the citys municipal taxes pursuant to alabama 1975 whereupon it shall be the duty of the county revenue commissioner to add the amounts of any weed andor trash lien to the next regular bills for taxes levied against the respective lots and parcels of land and thereafter any weed andor trash liens shall be collected at the same time and in the same manner as ordinary municipal ad valorem taxes are collected and shall be subject to the same penalties and the same procedure under foreclosure and sale in case of delinquency the county revenue commissioner shall retain ten percent of the amount of each weed andor trash lien collected and remit the remainder to the municipality the amount retained by the revenue commissioner shall be used for operational purposes art ii7 102097  art ii7 code comparative table  1974 code iii 3446 ch 74 art iii 3646 2125 362146 ch 58 art ii 3625115 3449 418a11 3449 1 updated  198626 zoning ordinance city of eufaula alabama an ordinance establishing comprehensive zoning regulations for the city of eufaula alabama and providing for the administration enforcement and amendment thereof in accordance with the provisions of the authority granted by code of alabama 197 sec 11521 et seq whereas alabama 197 et seq empowers the city of eufaula to enact a zoning ordinance and to provide for its administration enforcement and amendment and whereas the city council deems it necessary for the purpose of promoting the health safety morals and general welfare of the city to enact such an ordinance and whereas the city council has appointed the planning commission to recommend the boundaries of the various original districts and appropriate regulations to be enforced therein and whereas the planning commission has divided the city into districts and has prepared regulations pertaining to such districts in accordance with a comprehensive plan and designed to lessen congestion in the streets to secure safety from fire panic and other dangers to promote health and the general welfare to provide adequate light and air to prevent the overcrowding of land to avoid undue concentration of population to facilitate the adequate provision of transportation water sewerage schools parks and other public requirements and whereas the planning commission has given reasonable consideration among other things to the character of the districts and their peculiar suitability for particular uses with a view to conserving the value of buildings and encouraging the most appropriate use of land throughout the municipality and whereas the city council has given due public notice of hearings relating to zoning districts regulations and restrictions and has held such public hearings and whereas all requirements of alabama 197 et seq with regard to the preparation of the report of the planning commission and subsequent action of the city council have been met now therefore the public welfare requiring it be it ordained by the city council of eufaula alabama as follows attachments and supplements thereto shall be known as the eufaula zoning  official zoning map the city is hereby divided into zones or districts as shown on the official zoning map which together with all explanatory matter thereon is hereby adopted by reference and declared to be a part of this ordinance 131 the official zoning map shall be identified by the signature of the council president attested by the city clerk and bearing the seal of the city under the following words this is to certify that this is the official zoning map of the city of eufaula alabama together with the date of the adoption of this ordinance 132 if in accordance with the provisions of this ordinance changes are made in district boundaries or other matter portrayed on the official zoning map such changes shall be entered on the official zoning map promptly after the amendment has been approved by the city council with an entry on the official zoning map such changes shall be entered on the official zoning map as follows the new boundary line shall be drawn and within the newly zoned area a circle shall be drawn and include the designation of the new zone the ordinance number which approved the change and the effective date of the change such changes shall be completed by the city planner or a designee thereof 133 no changes of any nature shall be made on the official zoning map or matter shown thereon except in conformity with the procedures set forth in this ordinance any unauthorized change of whatever kind by any person or persons shall be considered a violation of this ordinance and punishable as provided under 34 regardless of the existence of purported copies of the official zoning map which may from time to time be made or published the official zoning map which shall be located in the eufaula zoning office at eufaula city hall shall be the final authority as to the current zoning status of land and water areas buildings and other structures in the city replacement of official zoning map in the event that the official zoning map becomes damaged destroyed lost or difficult to interpret because of the nature or number of changes and additions the city council may by resolution adopt a new official zoning map which shall supersede the prior official zoning map the new official zoning map may correct drafting or other errors or omissions in the prior official zoning map but no such correction shall have the effect of amending the original 6 official zoning map or any subsequent amendment thereof the new official zoning map shall be identified by the signature of the mayor attested by the city clerk and bearing the seal of the city under the following words this is to certify that this official zoning map supersedes and replaces the official zoning map adopted date of adoption of map being replaced as part of the zoning the city of eufaula alabama unless the prior official zoning map has been lost or has been totally destroyed the prior map or any significant parts thereof remaining shall be preserved together with all available records pertaining to its adoption or amendment 7 article two rules for interpretation of district boundaries boundary interpretations where uncertainty exists as to the boundaries of districts as shown on the official zoning map the following rules shall apply 211 boundaries indicated as approximately following the centerlines of streets highways or alleys shall be construed to follow such centerlines 212 boundaries indicated as approximately following platted lot lines shall be construed as following such lot lines 213 boundaries indicated as approximately following city limits shall be construed as following such city limits 214 boundaries indicated as following railroad lines shall be construed to be midway between the main tracks 215 boundaries indicated as following shore lines shall be construed to follow such shore lines and in the event of change in the shore line shall be construed as moving with the actual shore line  boundaries indicated as approximately following the center lines of streams rivers canals lakes or other bodies of water shall be construed to follow such center lines 216 boundaries indicated as parallel to or extensions of features indicated in subsections 211 above shall be so construed distances not specifically indicated on the official zoning map shall be determined by the scale of the map 217 where physical or cultural features existing on the ground are at variance with those shown on the official zoning map or in other circumstances not covered by subsections 211 above the board of adjustment shall interpret the district boundaries any party aggrieved by any final judgment or decision of said board of zoning adjustments may appeal said decision as provided for in alabama 197 18 where a district boundary line divides a lot which was in single ownership at the time of passage of this ordinance the board of adjustment may permit as a special exception the extension of the regulations for either portion of the lot 8 this page is intentionally left blank 9 article three application of district regulations particularly except as hereinafter provided 311 no building structure or land shall hereafter be used or occupied and no building or structure or part thereof shall hereafter be erected constructed reconstructed moved or structurally altered except in conformity with all of the regulations herein specified for the district in which it is located 312 no building or other structure shall hereafter be erected or altered  to exceed the height or bulk  to accommodate or house a greater number of families  to occupy a greater percentage of lot area  to have narrower or smaller rear yards front yards side yards or other open spaces than herein required or in any other manner contrary to the provisions of this ordinance 313 no part of a yard or other open space or offstreet parking or loading space required about or in connection with any building for the purpose of complying with this ordinance shall be included as part of a yard open space or offstreet parking or loading space similarly required for another building 314 no yard or lot existing at the time of passage of this ordinance shall be reduced in dimension or area below the minimum requirements set forth herein yards or lots created after the effective date of this ordinance shall meet at least the minimum requirements established by this ordinance 315 all territory which may hereafter be annexed to the city shall be
